##### **Detecting Trojaned DNNs via Spectral Regression Analysis**
2605.21146v1 by Samuele Pasini, Jinhan Kim, Paolo Tonella

Modern DNNs are repeatedly fine-tuned to incorporate new data and functionality. This evolutionary workflow introduces a security risk when updated data cannot be fully trusted, as adversaries may implant Trojans during fine-tuning. We present MIST, a Trojan detection approach that analyzes how a model's internal representations change during fine-tuning. Rather than attempting to reconstruct trigger conditions, MIST characterizes benign model evolution using pre-activation spectra and flags updates whose spectral deviations are inconsistent with this reference. This framing treats Trojan detection as a regression problem over model updates. An empirical evaluation across four datasets and eight Trojan attacks shows that spectral distances reliably distinguish Trojaned updates from clean fine-tuning. MIST outperforms state-of-the-art detection accuracy after a single update, without requiring any knowledge about the poisoned data or the trigger, and remains effective under multi-step benign evolution, with graceful and bounded degradation. These results indicate that spectral evolution provides a stable and assumption-light signal for detecting malicious model updates.

摘要：現代的深度神經網絡（DNN）會不斷進行微調，以納入新的數據和功能。當更新後的數據無法完全信任時，這種演變工作流程會引入安全風險，因為對手可能在微調過程中植入木馬。我們提出了MIST，一種木馬檢測方法，分析模型在微調過程中內部表示的變化。MIST並不試圖重建觸發條件，而是利用預激活光譜來描述良性模型的演變，並標記那些其光譜偏差與此參考不一致的更新。這種框架將木馬檢測視為模型更新的回歸問題。對四個數據集和八個木馬攻擊的實證評估顯示，光譜距離可靠地區分了木馬更新和乾淨的微調。MIST在單次更新後超越了最先進的檢測準確性，無需任何有關被污染數據或觸發器的知識，並在多步良性演變下保持有效，且退化平穩且有界限。這些結果表明，光譜演變提供了一個穩定且假設輕量的信號，用於檢測惡意模型更新。

##### **Winfree Oscillatory Neural Network**
2605.20922v1 by Jiawen Dai, Yue Song

Oscillations and synchronization are widely believed to play a fundamental role in representation and computation. However, existing machine learning approaches based on synchronization dynamics have largely been confined to specialized settings such as object discovery, with limited evidence of scalability to standard vision benchmarks or logic reasoning tasks. We propose the Winfree Oscillatory Neural Network (WONN), a dynamical neural architecture based on generalized Winfree dynamics. WONN evolves representations on the torus $(S^1)^d$ through structured oscillatory interactions, combining phase-based inductive biases with flexible and hierarchical interaction mechanisms instantiated as either fixed trigonometric mappings or learnable neural networks. We evaluate WONN on image recognition and complex reasoning tasks, including CIFAR, ImageNet, Maze-hard, and Sudoku. Across these domains, WONN achieves competitive or superior performance with strong parameter efficiency. In particular, WONN is, to our knowledge, the first synchronization-based oscillatory architecture to scale competitively to ImageNet-1K. Furthermore, on Maze-hard, WONN achieves 80.1% accuracy using only 1% of the parameters of prior state-of-the-art models. These results suggest that structured oscillatory dynamics provide a scalable and parameter-efficient alternative to conventional neural architectures.

摘要：振盪和同步被廣泛認為在表徵和計算中扮演著基本角色。<lb/>然而，現有基於同步動力學的機器學習方法主要局限於專門的環境，例如物體發現，對於標準視覺基準或邏輯推理任務的可擴展性證據有限。<lb/>我們提出了Winfree振盪神經網絡（WONN），這是一種基於廣義Winfree動力學的動態神經架構。<lb/>WONN通過結構化的振盪互動在圓環$(S^1)^d$上發展表徵，結合基於相位的歸納偏見與靈活的層次互動機制，這些機制可以是固定的三角函數映射或可學習的神經網絡。<lb/>我們在圖像識別和複雜推理任務上評估了WONN，包括CIFAR、ImageNet、Maze-hard和數獨。<lb/>在這些領域中，WONN實現了具有競爭力或更優的性能，並且參數效率高。<lb/>特別是，據我們所知，WONN是第一個能夠在ImageNet-1K上具有競爭力的基於同步的振盪架構。<lb/>此外，在Maze-hard上，WONN僅使用1%的參數便達到了80.1%的準確率，這是先前最先進模型的1%。<lb/>這些結果表明，結構化的振盪動力學為傳統神經架構提供了一種可擴展且參數高效的替代方案。

##### **Evaluating Speech Articulation Synthesis with Articulatory Phoneme Recognition**
2605.20920v1 by Vinicius Ribeiro, Yves Laprie

Recent advances in machine learning and the availability of articulatory datasets allow vocal tract synthesis to be conditioned on phonetic sequences, a primary task of articulatory speech synthesis. However, quality assessment needs a better definition. Generally, ranking generative models is tricky due to subjectivity. However, articulatory synthesis has the additional difficulty of requiring specialized knowledge in vocal tract anatomy and acoustics. To address this problem, this paper proposes to evaluate speech articulation synthesis using phoneme recognition as a proxy.
  Our hypothesis is that phoneme recognition using articulatory features better captures nuances in phoneme production, such as correct places of articulation, which traditional metrics (e.g., point-wise distance metrics) do not. We train a neural network with acoustic and articulatory features extracted from a single-speaker RT-MRI dataset. Then, we compare the recognition performance when testing the model with different synthetic articulatory features. Our results show that our articulatory feature set is phonetically rich and helps exploring additional dimensions on speech articulation synthesis.

摘要：最近在機器學習方面的進展以及發音數據集的可用性，使得聲道合成可以根據語音序列進行調整，這是發音語音合成的一項主要任務。<lb/>然而，質量評估需要更好的定義。<lb/>一般來說，對生成模型進行排名是棘手的，因為這涉及主觀性。<lb/>然而，發音合成還有額外的困難，因為它需要對聲道解剖學和聲學的專業知識。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，本文提出使用音素識別作為代理來評估語音發音合成。<lb/>我們的假設是，使用發音特徵的音素識別能更好地捕捉音素產生中的細微差別，例如正確的發音部位，而傳統的度量標準（例如，逐點距離度量）則無法做到這一點。<lb/>我們訓練了一個神經網絡，使用從單一講者的RT-MRI數據集中提取的聲學和發音特徵。<lb/>然後，我們比較了在使用不同合成發音特徵測試模型時的識別性能。<lb/>我們的結果顯示，我們的發音特徵集在語音上是豐富的，並有助於探索語音發音合成的其他維度。

##### **Sutra: Tensor-Op RNNs as a Compilation Target for Vector Symbolic Architectures**
2605.20919v1 by Emma Leonhart

Sutra is a typed, purely functional programming language whose compiled forward pass is a PyTorch neural network. The compiler beta-reduces the whole program -- primitives, control flow, string I/O -- to one fused tensor-op graph over a frozen embedding substrate. Rotation binding, unbind, bundle, polynomial Kleene three-valued logic, and tail-recursive loops all lower to tensor operations; the Kleene connectives are Lagrange-interpolated polynomials exact on the {-1, 0, +1} truth grid. Validation is one fact tested two ways. (1) The same program runs on four frozen embeddings spanning two modalities -- three text encoders (nomic-embed-text, all-minilm, mxbai-embed-large) and one protein language model (ESM-2) -- and decodes bundles at 100% accuracy through width k=8 on every substrate, where the textbook Hadamard product has already collapsed (2.5% on mxbai-embed-large, 7.5% on all-minilm). (2) PyTorch autograd flows through the actually compiled graph: a fuzzy-rule classifier written in .su trains from random init (18.7 +/- 9.5%; chance = 20%, five classes) to 100.0 +/- 0.0% (three seeds) by backpropagating through the emitted graph, the symbolic source unmodified. A weighted variant additionally trains a scalar cosine gain and writes it back into the .su source as a numeric literal; recompiling reproduces the trained behaviour to ~2e-7 per logit, so the trained model is itself legible, recompilable code. The same artifact is therefore both a logic program and a trainable neural network.

摘要：Sutra是一種類型化的純函數式編程語言，其編譯後的前向傳遞是一個PyTorch神經網絡。編譯器將整個程序進行β約簡——原始操作、控制流、字符串輸入/輸出——轉換為一個融合的張量操作圖，基於一個凍結的嵌入基底。旋轉綁定、解除綁定、捆綁、多項式克里尼三值邏輯和尾遞歸循環都降低為張量操作；克里尼連接詞是Lagrange插值多項式，在{-1, 0, +1}真值網格上精確。驗證是以兩種方式測試的同一事實。(1) 相同的程序在四個跨越兩種模態的凍結嵌入上運行——三個文本編碼器（nomic-embed-text、all-minilm、mxbai-embed-large）和一個蛋白質語言模型（ESM-2）——並且在每個基底上以100%的準確率解碼捆綁，寬度k=8，其中教科書的哈達瑪乘積已經崩潰（在mxbai-embed-large上為2.5%，在all-minilm上為7.5%）。(2) PyTorch自動微分流經實際編譯的圖：一個用.su編寫的模糊規則分類器從隨機初始化（18.7 +/- 9.5%；機會=20%，五個類別）訓練到100.0 +/- 0.0%（三個種子），通過反向傳播經過發出的圖，符號源未經修改。一個加權變體額外訓練一個標量餘弦增益，並將其寫回.su源作為數字文字；重新編譯再現訓練行為至約2e-7每logit，因此訓練出的模型本身是可讀的、可重新編譯的代碼。因此，這個相同的工件同時是邏輯程序和可訓練的神經網絡。

##### **Terminal-World: Scaling Terminal-Agent Environments via Agent Skills**
2605.20876v1 by Zihao Cheng, Hongru Wang, Zeming Liu, Xinyi Wang, Xiangrong Zhu, Yuhang Guo, Wei Lin, Jeff Z. Pan, Yunhong Wang

Terminal agents extend Large Language Models with the ability to execute tasks directly in command-line environments, but their progress is bottlenecked by the scarcity of high-quality training data. Existing approaches bootstrap from partial sources such as human-defined seeds or GitHub repositories to instantiate one component and then complete the rest, producing tasks confined to narrow seed distributions, environments misaligned with task semantics, and inefficient trajectories from unguided exploration. To address these limitations, we introduce Terminal-World, a fully automated pipeline that uses agent skills as the central synthesis primitive, which jointly encode what to accomplish, when to apply (preconditions and environment state), and how to execute, enabling task instructions, environments, and teacher trajectories to be co-derived. To further broaden the synthesis space, Terminal-World composes skills into skill teams and skill graphs for multi-role and cross-domain task synthesis. Using this pipeline, we construct 5,723 training environments and train Terminal-World-8B/14B/32B, evaluated across 6 benchmarks where the Terminal-World series consistently outperforms terminal-agent baselines. Notably, using the same teacher model and only 1.2% of the training data, Terminal-World-32B surpasses Nemotron-Terminal-32B on Terminal-Bench 2.0 by +4.5 Pass@1 (31.5) and achieves 43.8 Pass@3.

摘要：終端代理擴展了大型語言模型，使其能夠在命令行環境中直接執行任務，但其進展受到高品質訓練數據稀缺的瓶頸限制。現有的方法從部分來源（如人為定義的種子或 GitHub 倉庫）啟動，以實例化一個組件，然後完成其餘部分，產生受限於狹窄種子分佈的任務、與任務語義不對齊的環境以及來自無指導探索的低效軌跡。為了解決這些限制，我們引入了 Terminal-World，一個完全自動化的管道，使用代理技能作為中央合成原語，這些技能共同編碼要完成的任務、何時應用（前提條件和環境狀態）以及如何執行，從而使任務指令、環境和教師軌跡能夠共同推導。為了進一步擴大合成空間，Terminal-World 將技能組合成技能團隊和技能圖，以進行多角色和跨領域的任務合成。使用這個管道，我們構建了 5,723 個訓練環境並訓練了 Terminal-World-8B/14B/32B，並在 6 個基準測試中進行評估，其中 Terminal-World 系列始終超越終端代理基準。值得注意的是，使用相同的教師模型和僅 1.2% 的訓練數據，Terminal-World-32B 在 Terminal-Bench 2.0 上超越了 Nemotron-Terminal-32B，獲得了 +4.5 Pass@1（31.5）並達到 43.8 Pass@3。

##### **GraphRAG on Consumer Hardware: Benchmarking Local LLMs for Healthcare EHR Schema Retrieval**
2605.20815v1 by Peter Fernandes, Ria Kanjilal

Graph-based Retrieval Augmented Generation (GraphRAG) extends retrieval-augmented generation to support structured reasoning over complex corpora, but its reliability under resource-constrained, privacy-sensitive deployments remains unclear. In healthcare, where Electronic Health Record (EHR) data is complex and strictly regulated, reliance on cloud-based large language models (LLMs) introduces challenges in cost, latency, and compliance. In this work, we present a systematic evaluation of GraphRAG for EHR schema retrieval using locally deployed open-source LLMs. We implement the Microsoft GraphRAG pipeline on real-world EHR schema documentation and benchmark four models, including Llama 3.1 (8B), Mistral (7B), Qwen 2.5 (7B), and Phi-4-mini (3.8B), each deployed via Ollama on a single consumer GPU (8 GB VRAM). We evaluate indexing efficiency, knowledge graph construction, query latency, answer quality, and hallucination under both global and local retrieval modes. Our results reveal substantial differences: Llama 3.1 produces the richest knowledge graph (1,172 entities), Qwen 2.5 achieves the best answer quality (3.3/5), Phi-4-mini fails to complete the pipeline due to structured-output errors, and Mistral exhibits degenerate repetition behavior. We further show that GraphRAG exhibits a practical capacity threshold, where models below approximately 7B parameters fail to reliably produce valid structured outputs and cannot complete the pipeline. In addition, indexing and answer quality are decoupled across models, and local retrieval consistently outperforms global summarization in both latency and factual grounding, with reduced hallucination. These findings demonstrate that GraphRAG is feasible on consumer hardware while highlighting the importance of model selection and retrieval design for robust deployment in regulated settings.

摘要：Graph-based Retrieval Augmented Generation (GraphRAG) 擴展了檢索增強生成，以支持對複雜語料庫的結構化推理，但其在資源受限和隱私敏感的部署下的可靠性仍不明確。<lb/>在醫療保健領域，電子健康記錄 (EHR) 數據複雜且受到嚴格監管，依賴基於雲的大型語言模型 (LLMs) 在成本、延遲和合規性方面帶來挑戰。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們針對 EHR 架構檢索，使用本地部署的開源 LLMs 對 GraphRAG 進行系統評估。<lb/>我們在真實世界的 EHR 架構文檔上實施了 Microsoft GraphRAG 管道，並基準測試了四個模型，包括 Llama 3.1 (8B)、Mistral (7B)、Qwen 2.5 (7B) 和 Phi-4-mini (3.8B)，每個模型都通過 Ollama 在單個消費者 GPU (8 GB VRAM) 上部署。<lb/>我們評估了索引效率、知識圖譜構建、查詢延遲、答案質量和幻覺，並在全球和本地檢索模式下進行比較。<lb/>我們的結果顯示出顯著差異：Llama 3.1 產生了最豐富的知識圖譜 (1,172 個實體)，Qwen 2.5 實現了最佳答案質量 (3.3/5)，Phi-4-mini 由於結構化輸出錯誤未能完成管道，而 Mistral 則表現出退化重複行為。<lb/>我們進一步顯示 GraphRAG 具有實際的容量閾值，約 7B 參數以下的模型無法可靠地產生有效的結構化輸出，並且無法完成管道。<lb/>此外，索引和答案質量在模型之間是解耦的，本地檢索在延遲和事實基礎上始終優於全球摘要，並減少了幻覺。<lb/>這些發現表明 GraphRAG 在消費者硬體上是可行的，同時突顯了模型選擇和檢索設計在受監管環境中穩健部署的重要性。

##### **Tunable MAGMAX: Preference-Aware Model Merging for Continual Learning**
2605.20803v1 by Kei Hiroshima, Kento Uchida, Shinichi Shirakawa

Continual learning (CL) aims to train models sequentially on multiple tasks while mitigating catastrophic forgetting of previously learned knowledge. Recent advances in large pre-trained models (LPMs) and model merging techniques, such as MAGMAX, have demonstrated effective CL performance by combining task-specific parameters. However, existing methods primarily focus on average performance across all tasks and do not adequately address how to construct models accommodating different deployment environments or varying user preferences. This paper proposes a model merging framework, termed Tunable MAGMAX, which enables preference-aware control of task-specific performance in CL. Our method introduces a preference vector that controls the number of elements selected from each task vector during model merging, allowing us to adjust the merged model performance according to their deployment needs. We further propose a method for automatically constructing appropriate preference vectors by leveraging small amounts of target environment data and datasets from model training tasks, thereby eliminating the need for manual specification. The experimental result on CL benchmark tasks demonstrates that Tunable MAGMAX effectively controls task-wise performance and successfully adapts merged models to various target environments. The proposed Tunable MAGMAX achieves superior or comparable performance to baseline methods, making it a practical solution for deploying CL models to various environments where the preferences of each task performance differ.

摘要：持續學習（CL）旨在對多個任務進行順序訓練，同時減少對先前學習知識的災難性遺忘。最近在大型預訓練模型（LPMs）和模型合併技術（如MAGMAX）方面的進展，通過結合任務特定參數，展示了有效的CL性能。然而，現有方法主要集中在所有任務的平均性能上，並未充分解決如何構建適應不同部署環境或變化用戶偏好的模型。本文提出了一種名為可調MAGMAX的模型合併框架，該框架使得在CL中能夠根據偏好進行任務特定性能的控制。我們的方法引入了一個偏好向量，該向量控制在模型合併過程中從每個任務向量中選擇的元素數量，使我們能夠根據部署需求調整合併模型的性能。我們進一步提出了一種方法，通過利用少量目標環境數據和模型訓練任務的數據集，自動構建適當的偏好向量，從而消除手動指定的需求。在CL基準任務上的實驗結果表明，可調MAGMAX有效控制任務性能，並成功地將合併模型適應於各種目標環境。所提出的可調MAGMAX在性能上優於或可與基線方法相媲美，使其成為將CL模型部署到各種環境中，滿足每個任務性能偏好不同的實用解決方案。

##### **PACD-Net: Pseudo-Augmented Contrastive Distillation for Glycemic Control Estimation from SMBG**
2605.20751v1 by Canyu Lei, David Repaske, Jianxin Xie

Effective diabetes management requires continuous monitoring of glycemic levels. Clinically, glycemic control is assessed using metrics such as Time in Range (TIR), Time Below Range (TBR), and Time Above Range (TAR), typically derived from continuous glucose monitoring (CGM). However, many patients rely on self-monitoring of blood glucose (SMBG) due to the high cost and limited accessibility of CGM. Unlike CGM, SMBG provides sparse and irregular measurements, making accurate estimation of these metrics challenging. Conventional supervised learning approaches struggle under such sparsity, leading to poor generalization and unstable performance. To address this, we propose PACD-Net, a self-supervised contrastive knowledge distillation framework for estimating glycemic control from SMBG. Pseudo-SMBG samples with richer temporal coverage are used as teacher signals to guide learning from sparse observations. In addition, multi-view contrastive learning enforces representation consistency across diverse sampling patterns. The model adopts a hybrid Swin Transformer-CNN backbone to capture temporal dependencies in sparse SMBG sequences. Experimental results demonstrate that PACD-Net consistently outperforms existing methods in estimating TAR, TIR, and TBR from real-world SMBG data, achieving improved accuracy as well as enhanced stability and generalization under extremely sparse observation settings. The proposed framework provides a practical tool for clinical SMBG interpretation and offers a generalizable approach for learning from sparse and irregularly sampled sensor data in broader applications.

摘要：有效的糖尿病管理需要持續監測血糖水平。臨床上，血糖控制通常使用如範圍內時間（Time in Range, TIR）、範圍下時間（Time Below Range, TBR）和範圍上時間（Time Above Range, TAR）等指標來評估，這些指標通常來自持續血糖監測（Continuous Glucose Monitoring, CGM）。然而，許多患者因為CGM的高成本和有限的可及性而依賴自我監測血糖（Self-Monitoring of Blood Glucose, SMBG）。與CGM不同，SMBG提供稀疏且不規則的測量，使得準確估算這些指標變得具有挑戰性。傳統的監督學習方法在這種稀疏性下表現不佳，導致泛化能力差和性能不穩定。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了PACD-Net，一種自我監督對比知識蒸餾框架，用於從SMBG中估算血糖控制。使用具有更豐富時間覆蓋的偽SMBG樣本作為教師信號，以指導從稀疏觀測中學習。此外，多視角對比學習強化了不同取樣模式下的表示一致性。該模型採用混合的Swin Transformer-CNN骨幹，以捕捉稀疏SMBG序列中的時間依賴性。實驗結果表明，PACD-Net在從真實世界的SMBG數據中估算TAR、TIR和TBR方面始終優於現有方法，實現了更高的準確性以及在極度稀疏觀測條件下增強的穩定性和泛化能力。所提出的框架為臨床SMBG解讀提供了一個實用工具，並為在更廣泛的應用中從稀疏和不規則取樣的傳感器數據中學習提供了一種可泛化的方法。

##### **VBFDD-Agent for Electric Vehicle Battery Fault Detection and Diagnosis: Descriptive Text Modeling of Battery Digital Signals**

With the rapid proliferation of electric vehicles, the safety and reliability of lithium-ion batteries have become critical concerns. Traditional fault detection and diagnosis methods are usually designed for specific scenarios and predefined workflows, making them less effective in complex real-world applications.
  To address the scarcity of open-source battery fault report corpora and the lack of unified maintenance knowledge representation, this study proposes a descriptive text modeling approach for battery signal reports. ##### **Distribution-Aware Reward: Reinforcement Learning over Predictive Distributions for LLM Regression**
2605.20740v1 by Jungsoo Park, Hyungjoo Chae, Ethan Mendes, Jay DeYoung, Varsha Kishore, Wei Xu, Alan Ritter

Large language models can predict real-valued quantities from heterogeneous inputs such as text, code, and molecular strings, but most training objectives score each decoded floating-point number independently, improving point estimates without ensuring calibrated predictive distributions. This limits applications requiring candidate ranking or uncertainty estimation. We introduce Distribution-Aware Reward, an on-policy reinforcement learning objective whose main contribution is to train language models to produce better predictive distributions for regression tasks, rather than only optimizing individual decoded outputs against scalar targets. Our method treats multiple decoded samples as an empirical predictive distribution, evaluates it with the Continuous Ranked Probability Score, and assigns leave-one-out credit based on each rollout's marginal contribution to distribution quality, rewarding predictions that are both accurate and appropriately dispersed. We evaluate our method on a controlled Gaussian-mixture task, code performance prediction, and molecular property prediction from SMILES strings. Across tasks, our method improves over supervised fine-tuning and pointwise reinforcement learning baselines, with strong rank-correlation gains, including a 6-point Spearman improvement on KBSS. On MoleculeNet, it uses only SMILES strings yet remains competitive with strong graph-based and 3D molecular models. Further analyses show that our method mitigates rollout diversity collapse and improves uncertainty diagnostics, suggesting that directly optimizing predictive distributions makes language model regression more robust and better calibrated.

摘要：大型語言模型可以從異質輸入（如文本、代碼和分子字符串）中預測實數值量，但大多數訓練目標獨立評分每個解碼的浮點數，改善點估計卻不確保校準的預測分佈。這限制了需要候選排名或不確定性估計的應用。我們引入了分佈感知獎勵，這是一種政策內強化學習目標，其主要貢獻是訓練語言模型產生更好的回歸任務預測分佈，而不僅僅是針對標量目標優化單個解碼輸出。我們的方法將多個解碼樣本視為經驗預測分佈，使用連續排名概率分數進行評估，並根據每次回合對分佈質量的邊際貢獻分配留一法信用，獎勵既準確又適當分散的預測。我們在受控的高斯混合任務、代碼性能預測和從SMILES字符串中預測分子性質上評估我們的方法。在各項任務中，我們的方法優於監督微調和逐點強化學習基線，並且具有強大的排名相關性增益，包括在KBSS上提高6點的斯皮爾曼相關性。在MoleculeNet上，它僅使用SMILES字符串，但仍然與強大的基於圖形和3D分子模型競爭。進一步的分析顯示，我們的方法減輕了回合多樣性的崩潰並改善了不確定性診斷，這表明直接優化預測分佈使語言模型回歸更加穩健且更好地校準。

##### **Declarative Data Services: Structured Agentic Discovery for Composing Data Systems**
2605.20690v1 by Shanshan Ye, Duo Lu

Agentic discovery has shown that LLM-driven search can find novel algorithms, designs, and code under benchmark conditions. Translating the paradigm to multi-system data backends surfaces a harder problem: the search space is heterogeneous, the verifier is whether a deployed stack actually runs, and composition knowledge is unevenly captured in pretraining. Unbounded agentic discovery, a coding agent iterating on failure-log feedback, fails to converge consistently on a working stack even when iteration and explicit composition knowledge are added. We propose Declarative Data Services (DDS), an architecture for structured agentic discovery of data-system compositions from declarative user intent. The framework owns four typed contracts at successive layers (intent, operator DAG, per-system skills, runtime attribution) that decompose the global search into bounded sub-searches; sub-agents search each typed space, while the framework provides the channels by which knowledge flows forward as inline skill citations and errors route backward as typed signals. As a proof of life on a trading-backend workload, DDS converges where unbounded discovery does not; runtime failures become skill patches that the next deployment cites inline. We position this as an early prototype reporting lessons from real-world data-system composition.

摘要：代理發現顯示，基於大型語言模型的搜索可以在基準條件下找到新穎的算法、設計和代碼。將這一範式轉換為多系統數據後端則顯示出一個更棘手的問題：搜索空間是異質的，驗證器是已部署的堆棧是否實際運行，而組合知識在預訓練中捕獲得不均勻。無界限的代理發現，即一個基於失敗日誌反饋進行迭代的編碼代理，即使在添加迭代和明確的組合知識時，也無法一致地收斂到一個可行的堆棧。我們提出了聲明式數據服務（DDS），這是一種從聲明式用戶意圖中結構化代理發現數據系統組合的架構。該框架在連續層次上擁有四個類型的合約（意圖、運算符有向無環圖、每個系統的技能、運行時歸因），將全局搜索分解為有界的子搜索；子代理在每個類型的空間中進行搜索，而框架提供了知識向前流動的通道，作為內聯技能引用，錯誤則作為類型信號向後路由。作為交易後端工作負載的生命證明，DDS 在無界發現失敗的地方收斂；運行時故障成為下一次部署內聯引用的技能補丁。我們將此定位為一個早期原型，報告來自現實世界數據系統組合的經驗教訓。

##### **On the limits and opportunities of AI reviewers: Reviewing the reviews of Nature-family papers with 45 expert scientists**
2605.20668v1 by Seungone Kim, Dongkeun Yoon, Kiril Gashteovski, Juyoung Suk, Jinheon Baek, Pranjal Aggarwal, Ian Wu, Viktor Zaverkin, Spase Petkoski, Daniel R. Schrider, Ilija Dukovski, Francesco Santini, Biljana Mitreska, Yong Jeong, Kyeongha Kwon, Young Min Sim, Dragana Manasova, Arthur Porto, Biljana Mojsoska, Makoto Takamoto, Marko Shuntov, Ruoqi Liu, Hyunjoo Jenny Lee, Niyazi Ulas Dinç, Yehhyun Jo, Sunkyu Han, Chungwoo Lee, Huishan Li, Esther H. R. Tsai, Ergun Simsek, Khushboo Shafi, Yeonseung Chung, Jihye Park, Aleksandar Shulevski, Henrik Christiansen, Yoosang Son, Elly Knight, Amanda Montoya, Jeongyoun Ahn, Christian Langkammer, Heera Moon, Changwon Yoon, Nikola Stikov, Mooseok Jang, Edward Choi, Junhan Kim, Yeon Sik Jung, Woo Youn Kim, Jae Kyoung Kim, Ishraq Md Anjum, Hyun Uk Kim, Drew Bridges, Carolin Lawrence, Xiang Yue, Alice Oh, Akari Asai, Sean Welleck, Graham Neubig

With the advancement of AI capabilities, AI reviewers are beginning to be deployed in scientific peer review, yet their capability and credibility remain in question: many scientists simply view them as probabilistic systems without the expertise to evaluate research, while other researchers are more optimistic about their readiness without concrete evidence. Understanding what AI reviewers do well, where they fall short, and what challenges remain is essential. However, existing evaluations of AI reviewers have focused on whether their verdicts match human verdicts (e.g., score alignment, acceptance prediction), which is insufficient to characterize their capabilities and limits. In this paper, we close this gap through a large-scale expert annotation study, in which 45 domain scientists in Physical, Biological, and Health Sciences spent 469 hours rating 2,960 individual criticisms (each targeting one specific aspect of a paper) from human-written and AI-generated reviews of 82 Nature-family papers on correctness, significance, and sufficiency of evidence. On a composite of all three dimensions, a reviewing agent powered by GPT-5.2 scores above each paper's top-rated human reviewer (60.0% vs. 48.2%, p = 0.009), while all three AI reviewers (including Gemini 3.0 Pro and Claude Opus 4.5) exceed the lowest-rated human across every dimension. AI reviewers' accurate criticisms are also more often rated significant and well-evidenced, and surface a distinct 26% of issues no human raises. However, AI reviewers overlap far more than humans do (21% vs. 3% for cross-reviewer pairs), and exhibit 16 recurring weaknesses humans do not share, such as limited subfield knowledge, lack of long context management over multiple files, and overly critical stance on minor issues. Overall, our results position current AI reviewers as complements to, not substitutes for, human reviewers.

摘要：隨著人工智慧能力的進步，AI 評審者開始在科學同行評審中被部署，但它們的能力和可信度仍然受到質疑：許多科學家僅將其視為缺乏評估研究專業知識的概率系統，而其他研究人員則對其準備情況持較樂觀的態度，儘管缺乏具體證據。了解 AI 評審者擅長的地方、短板以及仍面臨的挑戰至關重要。然則，現有的 AI 評審者評估主要集中在其判決是否與人類判決相符（例如，分數一致性、接受預測），這不足以表徵其能力和限制。在本文中，我們通過一項大規模專家標註研究填補了這一空白，在該研究中，45 位物理、生物和健康科學領域的科學家花費 469 小時對 82 篇 Nature 系列論文中人類撰寫和 AI 生成的 2,960 條個別批評（每條針對論文的特定方面）進行評分，評估其正確性、重要性和證據的充分性。在所有三個維度的綜合評分中，由 GPT-5.2 驅動的評審代理的得分高於每篇論文的最高人類評審（60.0% 對 48.2%，p = 0.009），而所有三位 AI 評審者（包括 Gemini 3.0 Pro 和 Claude Opus 4.5）在每個維度上都超過了最低評分的人類。AI 評審者的準確批評也更常被評為重要且證據充分，並提出了 26% 的人類未提及的獨特問題。然而，AI 評審者的重疊程度遠超過人類（交叉評審者對的重疊率為 21% 對 3%），並表現出 16 種人類不具備的重複性弱點，例如有限的子領域知識、缺乏對多個文件的長期上下文管理，以及對小問題的過度批評。總體而言，我們的結果將當前的 AI 評審者定位為人類評審者的補充，而非替代品。

##### **REFLECTOR: Internalizing Step-wise Reflection against Indirect Jailbreak**
2605.20654v1 by Jiachen Ma, Jiawen Zhang, Xiangtian Li, Bo Zou, Chaochao Lu, Chao Yang

While Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate remarkable capabilities, they remain susceptible to sophisticated, multi-step jailbreak attacks that circumvent conventional surface-level safety alignment by exploiting the internal generation process. To address these vulnerabilities, we propose Reflector, a principled two-stage framework that internalizes self-reflection within the generation trajectory. Reflector first leverages teacher-guided generation to produce high-quality reflection data for supervised fine-tuning (SFT), establishing structured reflection patterns. It subsequently uses Reinforcement Learning (RL) with outcome-driven and reward-validity supervision to instill robust, autonomous self-reflection capabilities. Empirical results show that Reflector achieves Defense Success Rates (DSR) exceeding 90% against complex indirect attacks while generalizing robustly across diverse threat scenarios. Notably, the framework enhances both task-specific and general utility, yielding a 5.85% gain on GSM8K alongside improved performance on knowledge-intensive benchmarks. By internalizing trajectory-level safety, Reflector overcomes the fundamental limitations of surface alignment without significant computational overhead, offering an efficient and scalable solution for the development of safe and capable LLMs.

摘要：雖然大型語言模型（LLMs）展現出卓越的能力，但它們仍然容易受到複雜的多步驟越獄攻擊，這些攻擊通過利用內部生成過程來繞過傳統的表面安全對齊。為了解決這些脆弱性，我們提出了Reflector，一個原則性的兩階段框架，將自我反思內化於生成軌跡中。Reflector首先利用教師引導生成來產生高質量的反思數據，以進行監督式微調（SFT），建立結構化的反思模式。隨後，它使用強化學習（RL），結合以結果為驅動和獎勵有效性監督，來培養穩健的自主自我反思能力。實證結果顯示，Reflector在面對複雜間接攻擊時，防禦成功率（DSR）超過90%，同時在各種威脅場景中具有良好的泛化能力。值得注意的是，該框架增強了任務特定和一般實用性，GSM8K上獲得了5.85%的提升，並在知識密集型基準測試中表現改善。通過內化軌跡層級的安全性，Reflector克服了表面對齊的基本限制，且不需要顯著的計算開銷，為開發安全且有能力的LLMs提供了一個高效且可擴展的解決方案。

##### **Design for Manufacturing: A Manufacturability Knowledge-Integrated Reinforcement Learning Framework for Free-Form Pipe Routing in Aeroengines**
2605.20644v1 by Caicheng Wang, Zili Wang, Shuyou Zhang, Yongzhe Xiang, Zheyi Li, Liangyou Li, Jianrong Tan

Design for manufacturing plays a critical role in advanced aeroengine development, where complex components necessitate careful consideration of manufacturability. However, current practices in pipe routing remain largely decoupled from down-stream manufacturing, leading to labor-intensive, trial-and-error iterations to achieve manufacturable designs. To address this problem, this study proposes the Frenet-based pipe routing optimization (FPRO) framework, a manufacturability knowledge-integrated reinforcement learning approach for free-form pipe design in aeroengines. FPRO formulates the routing problem as a boundary value problem in the Frenet frame. In this framework, the pipe path is represented by curvature and torsion profiles, which are generated using cubic Hermite interpolation. To integrate design and manufacturing, domain-specific manufacturing knowledge is embedded as constraints on the permissible ranges of curvature and torsion. The path optimization is performed using the proximal policy optimization algorithm with stochastic exploration and a stage-guided reward mechanism. A unified mapping formulation then translates the optimized path into motion trajectories for the bending die, enabling direct fabrication on a six-axis free-bending machine. Experimental results demonstrate that FPRO consistently generates collision-free, manufacturable paths with smoother geometric profiles compared to Cartesian-based methods. It also achieves faster convergence and superior performance in terminal alignment, path length, obstacle avoidance, and manufacturability compared to state-of-the-art reinforcement learning baselines. Real-world validation confirms the close geometric correspondence between the manufactured pipe and its digital design, validating the practical feasibility of FPRO.

摘要：製造設計在先進航空發動機開發中扮演著關鍵角色，複雜的組件需要仔細考慮可製造性。<lb/>然而，目前的管道路由實踐在很大程度上與下游製造脫節，導致需要勞動密集型的試錯迭代來實現可製造的設計。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，本研究提出了基於Frenet的管道路由優化（FPRO）框架，這是一種將可製造性知識整合的強化學習方法，用於航空發動機中的自由形狀管道設計。<lb/>FPRO將路由問題表述為Frenet框架中的邊界值問題。<lb/>在這個框架中，管道路徑由曲率和扭轉剖面表示，這些剖面是使用三次Hermite插值生成的。<lb/>為了整合設計和製造，特定領域的製造知識被嵌入作為曲率和扭轉的允許範圍約束。<lb/>路徑優化是使用帶有隨機探索的近端策略優化算法和階段引導獎勵機制進行的。<lb/>然後，統一的映射公式將優化的路徑轉換為彎曲模具的運動軌跡，使得在六軸自由彎曲機上能夠直接製造。<lb/>實驗結果表明，FPRO與基於笛卡爾的方法相比，能夠持續生成無碰撞、可製造的路徑，且幾何剖面更平滑。<lb/>與最先進的強化學習基準相比，它在終端對齊、路徑長度、避障和可製造性方面也實現了更快的收斂和更優的性能。<lb/>現實世界的驗證確認了製造的管道與其數字設計之間的幾何對應性，驗證了FPRO的實際可行性。

##### **Trusted Weights, Treacherous Optimizations? Optimization-Triggered Backdoor Attacks on LLMs**
2605.20641v1 by Yifei Wang, Tianlin Li, Xiaohan Zhang, Yida Yang, Xiaoyu Zhang, Li Pan

Inference optimization is a vital technique for deploying LLMs at scale. Compilation is the most widely adopted optimization technique for LLMs. While it assumes semantic equivalence between the original and compiled graphs, we first uncover its numerical side effects can be maliciously exploited to implant stealthy backdoors in LLMs. We propose a unified optimization-triggered attack framework comprising two complementary strategies. Without any modification to the compiler or hardware, one strategy flips predictions for specific inputs only when the model is compiled, while the other uses a universal trigger that remains dormant under uncompiled execution but hijacks arbitrary inputs once compilation optimization is applied. Both attacks bypass standard safety evaluations run without compilation. We empirically demonstrate that these optimization-triggered backdoors achieve attack success rates averaging 90% across four mainstream open-source LLMs and four tasks, while clean accuracy is preserved at nearly 100% under all settings. Our findings reveal a novel attack surface at the intersection of optimization and security in the LLM deployment pipeline, and we investigate practical defenses to mitigate this threat.

摘要：推理優化是大規模部署LLM的重要技術。編譯是LLM中最廣泛採用的優化技術。雖然它假設原始圖和編譯圖之間存在語義等價，但我們首先揭示其數值副作用可能被惡意利用，以在LLM中植入隱秘的後門。我們提出了一個統一的優化觸發攻擊框架，包含兩種互補的策略。在不對編譯器或硬體進行任何修改的情況下，一種策略僅在模型被編譯時針對特定輸入翻轉預測，而另一種則使用一個通用觸發器，該觸發器在未編譯執行時保持靜默，但在應用編譯優化後劫持任意輸入。這兩種攻擊都能繞過未經編譯的標準安全評估。我們實證證明，這些優化觸發的後門在四個主流開源LLM和四個任務中達到了平均90%的攻擊成功率，而在所有設置下，清晰準確率幾乎保持在100%。我們的發現揭示了LLM部署管道中優化與安全交集處的一個新型攻擊面，並探討了實際防禦措施以減輕這一威脅。

##### **Divide-Prompt-Refine: a Training-Free, Structure-Aware Framework for Biomedical Abstract Generation**
2605.20628v1 by Sylvey Lin, Joe Menke, Shufan Ming, Dongin Nam, Neil Smalheiser, Halil Kilicoglu

Biomedical abstracts play a critical role in downstream NLP applications, such as information retrieval, biocuration, and biomedical knowledge discovery. However, a non-trivial number of biomedical articles do not have abstracts, diminishing the utility of these articles for downstream tasks. We propose DPR-BAG (Divide, Prompt, and Refine for Biomedical Abstract Generation), a training-free, zero-shot framework that generates coherent and factually grounded abstracts for biomedical articles with full text but no abstract. DPR-BAG decomposes full-text documents into structured rhetorical facets following the Background-Objective-Methods-Results-Conclusions (BOMRC) schema, performs parallel LLM-based summarization for each facet, and applies a final refinement stage to restore global discourse coherence. On PMC-MAD, a distribution-aligned dataset of 46,309 biomedical articles, DPR-BAG improves abstractive novelty over strong extractive and fine-tuned baselines, while maintaining factual consistency. Our ablation study reveals a counterintuitive finding: increasing prompt complexity or explicitly injecting entity-level guidance can degrade factual alignment, highlighting the importance of controlled prompting strategies. These findings underscore the potential of training-free, structure-aware frameworks for scalable biomedical abstract generation in low-resource settings. Our data and code are available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/pmc-mad/PMC-MAD and https://github.com/ScienceNLP-Lab/MultiTagger-v2/tree/main/DPR-BAG.

摘要：生物醫學摘要在下游自然語言處理應用中扮演著關鍵角色，例如信息檢索、生物策展和生物醫學知識發現。<lb/>然而，許多生物醫學文章並沒有摘要，這降低了這些文章在下游任務中的實用性。<lb/>我們提出了DPR-BAG（分割、提示和精煉生物醫學摘要生成），這是一個無需訓練的零-shot框架，能夠為具有完整文本但沒有摘要的生物醫學文章生成連貫且事實基礎的摘要。<lb/>DPR-BAG根據背景-目標-方法-結果-結論（BOMRC）架構將完整文本文件分解為結構化的修辭面，對每個面進行基於大型語言模型的並行總結，並應用最終的精煉階段以恢復全局話語的一致性。<lb/>在PMC-MAD上，這是一個包含46,309篇生物醫學文章的分佈對齊數據集，DPR-BAG在保持事實一致性的同時，改善了抽象新穎性，超越了強提取和微調基準。<lb/>我們的消融研究揭示了一個反直覺的發現：增加提示的複雜性或明確注入實體級指導可能會降低事實對齊，突顯了受控提示策略的重要性。<lb/>這些發現強調了無需訓練的、結構感知框架在低資源環境中可擴展生物醫學摘要生成的潛力。<lb/>我們的數據和代碼可在 https://huggingface.co/datasets/pmc-mad/PMC-MAD 和 https://github.com/ScienceNLP-Lab/MultiTagger-v2/tree/main/DPR-BAG 獲得。

##### **COAgents: Multi-Agent Framework to Learn and Navigate Routing Problems Search Space**
2605.20618v1 by Oleksandr Yakovenko, Mahdi Mostajabdaveh, Cheikh Ahmed, Abdullah Ali Sivas, Xiaorui Li, Zirui Zhou, Mao Kun

Although Vehicle Routing Problems (VRP) are essential to many real-world systems, they remain computationally intractable at scale due to their combinatorial complexity. Traditional heuristics rely on handcrafted rules for local improvements and occasional \textit{jumps} to escape local minima, but often struggle to generalize across diverse instances. We introduce \textbf{COAgents}, a cooperative multi-agent framework that models the search process as a graph: nodes represent solutions, and edges correspond to either local refinements or large perturbations for diversification (i.e., jumps). A \textit{Partial Search Graph} (PSG) is dynamically constructed during search, enabling COAgents to train a Node Selection Agent and a Move Selection Agent to guide intensification, and a Jump Agent to trigger well-timed explorations of new regions. Unlike end-to-end learning approaches, COAgents cleanly separates problem-agnostic search control from compact domain-specific encoding, facilitating adaptability across tasks. Extensive experiments on the CVRP and VRPTW benchmarks show that COAgents remains competitive with several learn-to-search baselines on CVRP and sets a new state of the art among learning-based methods on the more challenging VRPTW instances, reducing the gap to the best-known solutions by 14\% at $N\!=\!100$ and 44\% at $N\!=\!50$ relative to the strongest neural solver (POMO), and by 21\% and 40\% respectively relative to ALNS.
  Code is available at https://github.com/mahdims/COAgents.

摘要：儘管車輛路由問題（VRP）對許多現實世界系統至關重要，但由於其組合複雜性，在大規模下仍然計算上不可處理。傳統的啟發式方法依賴於手工製作的規則進行局部改進和偶爾的\textit{跳躍}以逃脫局部最小值，但往往難以在多樣的實例中進行泛化。我們介紹\textbf{COAgents}，一個合作的多代理框架，將搜索過程建模為圖：節點代表解，邊緣對應於局部精煉或大型擾動以實現多樣化（即，跳躍）。在搜索過程中動態構建\textit{部分搜索圖}（PSG），使COAgents能夠訓練一個節點選擇代理和一個移動選擇代理來引導強化，以及一個跳躍代理來觸發對新區域的適時探索。與端到端學習方法不同，COAgents清晰地將問題無關的搜索控制與緊湊的領域特定編碼分開，促進了跨任務的適應性。在CVRP和VRPTW基準上的廣泛實驗表明，COAgents在CVRP上仍然與幾個學習搜索基準保持競爭力，並在更具挑戰性的VRPTW實例中設立了學習方法的新最先進水平，相較於最強的神經解算器（POMO），在$N\!=\!100$時將與已知最佳解的差距縮小了14\%，在$N\!=\!50$時縮小了44\%，相對於ALNS則分別縮小了21\%和40\%。<lb/>代碼可在https://github.com/mahdims/COAgents獲得。

##### **Auto-Dreamer: Learning Offline Memory Consolidation for Language Agents**
2605.20616v1 by Chongrui Ye, Yuxiang Liu, Yu Wang, Haofei Yu, Yining Zhao, Ge Liu, Julian McAuley, Jiaxuan You

Language agents increasingly operate over streams of related tasks, yet existing memory systems struggle to convert accumulated experience into reusable knowledge. Retrieval-augmented and structured memory methods record per-session observations effectively, but often couple acquisition and consolidation into a single online process, leaving the agent without a global view across sessions to discover recurring patterns, abstract shared procedures, or prune redundant entries. Inspired by complementary learning systems theory, we propose Auto-Dreamer, a learned offline consolidator for language-agent memory. Auto-Dreamer decouples fast per-session memory acquisition from slow cross-session consolidation. Given a selected working region of a typed memory bank, the consolidator treats the region as read-only evidence, performs bounded tool-use to inspect entries and provenance-linked source trajectories, and synthesizes a fresh compact replacement set that abstracts across sessions and supersedes the original region. We train Auto-Dreamer via GRPO, using end-to-end agent performance as the reward signal to learn how to consolidate memories acquired through fast online experience. Trained on ScienceWorld trajectories alone, Auto-Dreamer outperforms fixed, RL-trained, and prompted memory baselines on ScienceWorld by 7 points while using an active memory bank 12$\times$ smaller than the strongest baseline, and continues to lead on held-out ALFWorld and WebArena without retraining -- using 6$\times$ less memory than the strongest baseline on ALFWorld.

摘要：語言代理人越來越多地在相關任務的流中運作，但現有的記憶系統在將累積的經驗轉化為可重用的知識方面面臨困難。檢索增強和結構化記憶方法有效地記錄每次會話的觀察，但通常將獲取和鞏固結合為單一的在線過程，導致代理人無法在會話之間獲得全球視野，以發現重複模式、抽象共享程序或修剪冗餘條目。受到互補學習系統理論的啟發，我們提出了 Auto-Dreamer，一種用於語言代理記憶的學習離線鞏固器。Auto-Dreamer 將快速的每次會話記憶獲取與緩慢的跨會話鞏固解耦。給定一個選定的類型記憶庫的工作區域，鞏固器將該區域視為只讀證據，執行有限的工具使用來檢查條目和來源鏈接的源軌跡，並綜合出一個新的緊湊替代集，該集跨會話抽象並取代原始區域。我們通過 GRPO 訓練 Auto-Dreamer，使用端到端代理性能作為獎勵信號，以學習如何鞏固通過快速在線經驗獲得的記憶。僅在 ScienceWorld 軌跡上訓練的 Auto-Dreamer，在 ScienceWorld 上的表現超過了固定的、強化學習訓練的和提示的記憶基準 7 分，同時使用的活動記憶庫比最強基準小 12$\times$，並且在未重新訓練的情況下，繼續在保留的 ALFWorld 和 WebArena 上領先——在 ALFWorld 上使用的記憶比最強基準少 6$\times$。

##### **From Automated to Autonomous: Hierarchical Agent-native Network Architecture (HANA)**
2605.20608v1 by Binghan Wu, Shoufeng Wang, Yunxin Liu, Ya-Qin Zhang, Joseph Sifakis, Ye Ouyang

Realizing Level 4/5 Autonomous Networks (AN) demands a shift from static automation to agent-native intelligence. Current operations, reliant on rigid scripts, lack the cognitive agency to handle off-nominal conditions. To address this, this letter proposes a hierarchical multi-agent reference architecture enabling high-level autonomy. The framework features a Dual-Driven Orchestrator that coordinates specialized Executive Agents, supported by a shared Public Memory for unified domain knowledge. A key innovation is the integration of agent self-awareness, which empowers the system to harmonize deliberative strategic governance with reflexive fault recovery. ##### **High Quality Embeddings for Horn Logic Reasoning**
2605.20467v1 by Yifan Zhang, Yasir White, Dean Clark, Joseph Sanchez, Jevon Lipsey, Ashely Hirst, Jeff Heflin

Neural networks can be trained to rank the choices made by logical reasoners, resulting in more efficient searches for answers. A key step in this process is creating useful embeddings, i.e., numeric representations of logical statements. This paper introduces and evaluates several approaches to creating embeddings that result in better downstream results. We train embeddings using triplet loss, which requires examples consisting of an anchor, a positive example, and a negative example. We introduce three ideas: generating anchors that are more likely to have repeated terms, generating positive and negative examples in a way that ensures a good balance between easy, medium, and hard examples, and periodically emphasizing the hardest examples during training. We conduct several experiments to evaluate this approach, including a comparison of different embeddings across different knowledge bases, in an attempt to identify what characteristics make an embedding well-suited to a particular reasoning task.

摘要：神經網絡可以被訓練來對邏輯推理者所做的選擇進行排名，從而實現更有效的答案搜尋。這一過程中的一個關鍵步驟是創建有用的嵌入，即邏輯陳述的數字表示。本文介紹並評估了幾種創建嵌入的方法，這些方法能夠產生更好的下游結果。我們使用三元組損失來訓練嵌入，這需要由一個錨點、一個正例和一個負例組成的示例。我們提出了三個想法：生成更可能包含重複術語的錨點，以確保在簡單、中等和困難示例之間保持良好的平衡的方式生成正例和負例，以及在訓練過程中定期強調最困難的示例。我們進行了幾個實驗來評估這種方法，包括比較不同知識庫中的不同嵌入，試圖確定哪些特徵使得嵌入適合特定的推理任務。

##### **Consistently Informative Soft-Label Temperature for Knowledge Distillation**
2605.20357v1 by Hoang-Chau Luong, Nghia Van Vo, Kaiqi Zhao, Lingwei Chen

Knowledge distillation (KD) transfers knowledge from a high-capacity teacher to a compact student by matching their predictive distributions, with temperature scaling serving as a central mechanism for smoothing teacher predictions and exposing informative "dark knowledge" beyond the hard label. However, the standard fixed-temperature design is inherently sample-agnostic. Since samples differ in logit scale and learning difficulty, a single global temperature produces teacher soft labels with highly inconsistent entropy: some predictions remain overly sharp and provide limited inter-class information, whereas others become over-smoothed and lose class-discriminative information. Moreover, sharing the same temperature between teacher and student further imposes rigid logit-scale alignment despite their capacity mismatch. To address these limitations, we propose CIST (Consistently Informative Soft-label Temperature), which assigns separate sample-wise adaptive temperatures to the teacher and student. This design produces consistently informative teacher soft labels while relaxing rigid teacher--student logit-scale matching. It also reweights the distillation objective according to teacher confidence and student learning difficulty. Theoretically, we show that teacher-label entropy is largely governed by the ratio between the maximum teacher logit and the temperature, providing a principled basis for adaptive smoothing. Empirically, CIST mitigates the inconsistency induced by fixed temperature, and experiments on both vision and language distillation tasks show consistent improvements over standard KD and strong baselines with negligible computational overhead.

摘要：知識蒸餾（KD）通過匹配高容量教師和緊湊學生的預測分佈來轉移知識，溫度縮放作為平滑教師預測和揭示超越硬標籤的資訊性「黑暗知識」的核心機制。然而，標準的固定溫度設計本質上是樣本無關的。由於樣本在邏輯尺度和學習難度上有所不同，單一的全局溫度會產生具有高度不一致熵的教師軟標籤：某些預測保持過於尖銳，提供有限的類間信息，而其他預測則過度平滑，失去類別區分信息。此外，教師和學生之間共享相同的溫度進一步強加了剛性的邏輯尺度對齊，儘管它們的能力不匹配。為了解決這些限制，我們提出了CIST（持續資訊性軟標籤溫度），它為教師和學生分配單獨的樣本自適應溫度。這種設計產生了一致的資訊性教師軟標籤，同時放鬆了剛性的教師-學生邏輯尺度匹配。它還根據教師信心和學生學習難度重新加權蒸餾目標。在理論上，我們表明教師標籤熵主要受最大教師邏輯與溫度之比的影響，為自適應平滑提供了原則基礎。在實證上，CIST減輕了固定溫度引起的不一致性，並且在視覺和語言蒸餾任務上的實驗顯示出相對於標準KD和強基準的一致性改進，且計算開銷微不足道。

##### **ClinSeekAgent: Automating Multimodal Evidence Seeking for Agentic Clinical Reasoning**
2605.20176v1 by Juncheng Wu, Letian Zhang, Yuhan Wang, Haoqin Tu, Hardy Chen, Zijun Wang, Cihang Xie, Yuyin Zhou

Large language models (LLMs) and agentic systems have shown promise for clinical decision support, but existing works largely assume that evidence has already been curated and handed to the model. Real-world clinical workflows instead require agents to actively seek, iteratively plan, and synthesize multimodal evidence from heterogeneous sources. In this paper, we introduce ClinSeekAgent, an automated agentic framework for dynamic multimodal evidence seeking that shifts the paradigm from passive evidence consumption to active evidence acquisition. Given only a clinical query and access to raw data sources, ClinSeekAgent gathers evidence by querying medical knowledge bases, navigating raw EHRs, and invoking medical imaging tools; refines its hypotheses as new information emerges; and integrates the collected evidence into grounded clinical decisions. ClinSeekAgent serves both as an inference-time agent for frontier LLMs and as a training-time pipeline for distilling high-quality agent trajectories into compact open-source models. To validate its inference-time effectiveness, we construct ClinSeek-Bench, which pairs Curated Input reasoning from fixed pre-selected evidence with Automated Evidence-Seeking over raw clinical data. On text-only EHR tasks, ClinSeekAgent improves Claude Opus 4.6 from 60.0 to 63.2 overall F1 and MiniMax M2.5 from 43.1 to 47.3, with positive risk-prediction gains in 7 out of 9 evaluated host models. On multimodal tasks, ClinSeekAgent improves Claude Opus 4.6 from 47.5 to 62.6 (+15.1); all evaluated models improve across the three CXR-related task groups. We further validate ClinSeekAgent as a training pipeline by distilling agentic evidence-seeking trajectories into ClinSeek-35B-A3B, which achieves 34.0 average F1 on existing AgentEHR-Bench, improving over its Qwen3.5-35B-A3B baseline by +11.9 points and approaching Claude Opus 4.6.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）和代理系統在臨床決策支持方面顯示出潛力，但現有的研究大多假設證據已經被整理並交給模型。實際的臨床工作流程則要求代理主動尋找、迭代計劃，並從異質來源綜合多模態證據。在本文中，我們介紹了ClinSeekAgent，一個自動化的代理框架，用於動態多模態證據尋求，將範式從被動的證據消耗轉變為主動的證據獲取。僅根據臨床查詢和對原始數據來源的訪問，ClinSeekAgent通過查詢醫療知識庫、導航原始電子健康記錄（EHR）和調用醫療影像工具來收集證據；隨著新信息的出現，不斷完善其假設；並將收集到的證據整合為有根據的臨床決策。ClinSeekAgent既作為前沿LLMs的推理時代理，也作為訓練時管道，用於將高質量的代理軌跡提煉成緊湊的開源模型。為了驗證其推理時的有效性，我們構建了ClinSeek-Bench，將固定預選證據的整理輸入推理與對原始臨床數據的自動證據尋求配對。在僅文本的EHR任務中，ClinSeekAgent將Claude Opus 4.6的整體F1從60.0提高到63.2，將MiniMax M2.5從43.1提高到47.3，在9個評估的主機模型中，有7個模型的風險預測獲得了正向增益。在多模態任務中，ClinSeekAgent將Claude Opus 4.6的分數從47.5提高到62.6（+15.1）；所有評估的模型在三個與CXR相關的任務組中均有所改善。我們進一步通過將代理證據尋求軌跡提煉成ClinSeek-35B-A3B來驗證ClinSeekAgent作為訓練管道的有效性，該模型在現有的AgentEHR-Bench上達到34.0的平均F1，較其Qwen3.5-35B-A3B基準提高了+11.9點，並接近Claude Opus 4.6。

##### **KoRe: Compact Knowledge Representations for Large Language Models**
2605.20170v1 by Davide Cavicchini, Fausto Giunchiglia, Jacopo Staiano

Modern Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown impressive performances in user-facing tasks such as question answering, as well as consistent improvements in reasoning capabilities. Still, the way these models encode knowledge seems inherently flawed: by design, LLMs encode world-knowledge within their parameters. This way of representing knowledge is inherently opaque, difficult to debug and update, and prone to hallucinations. On the other hand, Knowledge Graphs can provide human-readable and easily editable world knowledge representations, and their application in knowledge-intensive tasks has consistently proven beneficial to downstream performance. Nonetheless, current integration techniques require extensive retraining or finetuning. To overcome this issue, we introduce KoRe, a methodology to encode 1-hop sub-graphs into compact discrete knowledge tokens and inject them into a LLM backbone. We test the proposed approach on three established benchmarks, and report competitive performances coupled with a significant reduction (up to 10x) in token usage. Our results show that compact discrete KG representations can efficiently and effectively be used to ground modern LLMs.

摘要：現代大型語言模型（LLMs）在用戶面向的任務中，如問題回答，展現了令人印象深刻的表現，並且在推理能力上持續改進。儘管如此，這些模型編碼知識的方式似乎固有缺陷：根據設計，LLMs 在其參數中編碼世界知識。這種表示知識的方式本質上是不透明的，難以調試和更新，並且容易出現幻覺。另一方面，知識圖譜可以提供人類可讀且易於編輯的世界知識表示，並且在知識密集型任務中的應用一貫證明對下游性能有益。儘管如此，當前的整合技術需要大量的重新訓練或微調。為了解決這個問題，我們介紹了 KoRe，一種將 1-hop 子圖編碼為緊湊的離散知識標記並注入到 LLM 主幹中的方法。我們在三個已建立的基準上測試了所提出的方法，並報告了具有競爭力的表現，並顯著減少了（高達 10 倍）標記的使用。我們的結果顯示，緊湊的離散 KG 表示可以有效且高效地用於支持現代 LLMs。

##### **k-Inductive Neural Barrier Certificates for Unknown Nonlinear Dynamics**
2605.20108v1 by Ben Wooding, Hongchao Zhang, Taylor T. Johnson, Abolfazl Lavaei

While conventional (k=1) discrete-time barrier certificate conditions impose strict safety constraints by requiring the function to be non-increasing at every step, k-inductive barrier certificates relax this by allowing a temporary increase -- up to k-1 times, each within a threshold $ε$ -- while maintaining overall safety, and improving flexibility. This paper leverages neural networks and constructs k-inductive neural barrier certificates (k-NBCs) for (partially) unknown nonlinear systems. While neural networks offer scalability in the design process, they lack formal guarantees, requiring additional approaches such as counterexample-guided inductive synthesis (CEGIS) with satisfiability modulo theories (SMT) for verification. However, the CEGIS-SMT framework requires knowledge of system dynamics, which is unavailable in practical settings. To address this, we leverage the generalization of the Willems et al.'s fundamental lemma, using a single state trajectory, to construct a data-driven representation of (partially) unknown models for SMT verification without sacrificing accuracy. Additionally, CEGIS-SMT further removes the constraint of restricting barrier certificates to specific function classes, such as sum-of-squares, enabling greater flexibility in their design. We validate our approach on three nonlinear case studies with (partially) unknown dynamics.

摘要：傳統的 (k=1) 離散時間障礙證明條件通過要求函數在每一步都非遞增來施加嚴格的安全約束，而 k-歸納障礙證明則通過允許臨時增加（最多 k-1 次，每次在閾值 $ε$ 內）來放寬這一要求，同時保持整體安全性並提高靈活性。本文利用神經網絡，為（部分）未知的非線性系統構建 k-歸納神經障礙證明 (k-NBCs)。雖然神經網絡在設計過程中提供了可擴展性，但它們缺乏正式的保證，這需要額外的方法，例如帶有可滿足性模組理論 (SMT) 的反例引導歸納合成 (CEGIS) 來進行驗證。然而，CEGIS-SMT 框架需要對系統動力學的了解，而這在實際環境中是不可用的。為了解決這個問題，我們利用 Willems 等人的基本引理的推廣，使用單一狀態軌跡，構建了一個數據驅動的（部分）未知模型的 SMT 驗證表示，而不犧牲準確性。此外，CEGIS-SMT 進一步消除了將障礙證明限制於特定函數類別（如平方和）的約束，從而在設計上提供了更大的靈活性。我們在三個具有（部分）未知動力學的非線性案例研究中驗證了我們的方法。

##### **What Do Evolutionary Coding Agents Evolve?**
2605.20086v1 by Nico Pelleriti, Sree Harsha Nelaturu, Zhanke Zhou, Zongze Li, Max Zimmer, Bo Han, Sebastian Pokutta

Recent work pairs LLMs with evolutionary search to iteratively generate, modify, and select code using task-specific feedback. These systems have produced strong results in mathematical discovery and algorithm design, yet a fundamental question remains: what do they actually evolve? Progress is typically summarized by the best score a run reaches under a task-specific evaluator, but that score can reflect several different mechanisms: new algorithmic structure, re-tuning an existing strategy, recombining ideas already in the model's internal knowledge, or overfitting to the evaluator. Distinguishing these mechanisms requires inspecting the search process itself, not only its final outcome. We introduce EvoTrace, a dataset of evolutionary coding traces spanning four evolutionary frameworks, reasoning and non-reasoning models, and 16 tasks across mathematics and algorithm design. To analyze these traces, we develop EvoReplay, a replay-based methodology that reconstructs the local search states behind high-scoring solutions and tests controlled interventions, including adjusting constants, removing program components and substituting models or prompting contexts. We annotate every code edit in EvoTrace with one of nine recurring edit types using an LLM-as-judge pipeline validated against blind human re-annotation. Across EvoTrace, most score gains come from a small subset of these edit types. We further find a deterministic cycling pattern: about 30% of code lines added during search are byte-identical re-introductions of previously-deleted lines, present throughout nearly every run. These results show that benchmark gains in evolutionary coding agents can arise from qualitatively different mechanisms, only some of which correspond to new algorithmic structure. EvoTrace enables more diagnostic evaluation of evolutionary coding agents beyond final benchmark scores.

摘要：最近的研究將大型語言模型（LLMs）與進化搜索相結合，通過任務特定的反饋迭代生成、修改和選擇代碼。這些系統在數學發現和算法設計方面取得了強勁的成果，但仍然存在一個根本性問題：它們實際上在進化什麼？進展通常通過運行在任務特定評估器下達到的最佳分數來總結，但該分數可以反映幾種不同的機制：新的算法結構、重新調整現有策略、重新組合已在模型內部知識中的想法，或對評估器的過擬合。區分這些機制需要檢查搜索過程本身，而不僅僅是其最終結果。我們介紹了EvoTrace，這是一個跨越四個進化框架、推理和非推理模型，以及數學和算法設計中的16個任務的進化編碼痕跡數據集。為了分析這些痕跡，我們開發了EvoReplay，一種基於回放的方法論，重建高分解決方案背後的局部搜索狀態並測試控制干預，包括調整常數、刪除程序組件和替換模型或提示上下文。我們使用經過盲人重新註釋驗證的LLM作為評判者的管道，對EvoTrace中的每個代碼編輯進行了九種類型的重複編輯類型的註釋。在EvoTrace中，大多數分數增益來自這些編輯類型的一小部分。我們進一步發現了一種確定性循環模式：在搜索過程中添加的約30%的代碼行是之前刪除行的字節相同的重新引入，幾乎在每次運行中都存在。這些結果顯示，進化編碼代理的基準增益可以來自質量不同的機制，其中只有一部分與新的算法結構相對應。EvoTrace使得對進化編碼代理的診斷評估超越了最終基準分數。

##### **Text-to-SPARQL Generation with Reinforcement Learning: A GRPO-based Approach on DBLP**
2605.20066v1 by Jann Pfeifer, Debayan Banerjee, Ricardo Usbeck

Knowledge graph question answering seeks to translate natural language questions into executable queries over knowledge graphs, but existing approaches often rely on large models or full supervision in the form of gold query annotations. This study examines whether reinforcement learning with outcome-based rewards can train a small instruction-tuned language model to perform zero-shot Text-to-SPARQL generation in the scholarly domain. Group-Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) is applied to the Qwen3-1.7B model on DBLP-QuAD, using prompts that combine natural language questions with symbolic hints about entities and relations. Training relies on execution feedback, structural constraints, and answer-level rewards, with an additional variant that incorporates gold-query-based shaping. The resulting models are compared to the unmodified zero-shot baseline and to a supervised DoRA-finetuned baseline across answer-level accuracy, execution accuracy, category-wise scores, and generalization to held-out templates. GRPO substantially improves over the zero-shot baseline and exhibits competitive generalization, while supervised DoRA finetuning achieves higher overall accuracy on the same model scale. Ablation analyses indicate that execution-based rewards account for most gains, with additional shaping yielding limited additional benefit, suggesting that outcome-based reinforcement learning is a viable training strategy when gold queries are unavailable for token-level supervision.

摘要：知識圖譜問答旨在將自然語言問題轉換為可在知識圖譜上執行的查詢，但現有的方法通常依賴於大型模型或以金標註的形式進行完全監督。這項研究探討了基於結果的獎勵的強化學習是否可以訓練一個小型的指令調整語言模型，以在學術領域執行零-shot Text-to-SPARQL 生成。將群體相對政策優化（GRPO）應用於 Qwen3-1.7B 模型在 DBLP-QuAD 上，使用結合自然語言問題與有關實體和關係的符號提示的提示。訓練依賴於執行反饋、結構約束和答案級獎勵，還有一個額外變體納入了基於金標的塑形。所產生的模型與未修改的零-shot 基線以及經監督的 DoRA 微調基線進行比較，評估指標包括答案級準確性、執行準確性、類別得分和對保留模板的泛化能力。GRPO 在零-shot 基線上顯著提升，並展現出競爭性的泛化能力，而經監督的 DoRA 微調在相同模型規模上實現了更高的整體準確性。消融分析表明，基於執行的獎勵佔據了大部分增益，而額外的塑形僅帶來有限的額外好處，這表明當金標查詢無法用於標記級監督時，基於結果的強化學習是一種可行的訓練策略。

##### **PromptRad: Knowledge-Enhanced Multi-Label Prompt-Tuning for Low-Resource Radiology Report Labeling**
2605.20052v2 by Ying-Jia Lin, Tzu-Chin Lo, Ping-Chien Li, Chi-Tung Cheng, Chien-Hung Liao, Hung-Yu Kao

Automatic report labeling facilitates the identification of clinical findings from unstructured text and enables large-scale annotation for medical imaging research. Existing rule-based labelers struggle with the diverse descriptions in clinical reports, while fine-tuning pre-trained language models (PLMs) requires large amounts of labeled data that are often unavailable in clinical settings. In this paper, we propose PromptRad, a knowledge-enhanced multi-label \textbf{prompt}-tuning approach for \textbf{rad}iology report labeling under low-resource settings. PromptRad reformulates multi-label classification as masked language modeling and incorporates synonyms from the UMLS Metathesaurus into a multi-word verbalizer to enrich category representations. By fine-tuning the PLM without additional classification layers, PromptRad requires substantially less labeled data than conventional fine-tuning. Experiments on liver CT (computed tomography) reports show that PromptRad outperforms dictionary-based and fine-tuning baselines with only 32 labeled training examples, and achieves competitive performance with GPT-4 despite using a much smaller model. Further analysis demonstrates that PromptRad captures complex negation patterns more effectively than existing methods, making it a promising solution for report labeling in data-scarce clinical scenarios. Our code is available at https://github.com/ila-lab/PromptRad.

摘要：自動報告標記促進了從非結構化文本中識別臨床發現的能力，並使醫學影像研究的大規模註釋成為可能。現有的基於規則的標記器在臨床報告中面對多樣化的描述時表現不佳，而微調預訓練語言模型（PLMs）則需要大量標記數據，而這些數據在臨床環境中往往無法獲得。在本文中，我們提出了PromptRad，一種在低資源環境下用於放射科報告標記的知識增強多標籤\textbf{提示}微調方法。PromptRad將多標籤分類重新表述為掩蔽語言建模，並將UMLS Metathesaurus中的同義詞納入多詞語言化器中，以豐富類別表示。通過在不增加額外分類層的情況下微調PLM，PromptRad所需的標記數據遠少於傳統微調。對肝臟CT（計算機斷層掃描）報告的實驗表明，PromptRad在僅使用32個標記訓練樣本的情況下，超越了基於字典和微調的基準，並且儘管使用的模型小得多，仍能與GPT-4達到競爭性表現。進一步分析顯示，PromptRad比現有方法更有效地捕捉複雜的否定模式，使其成為數據稀缺臨床場景中報告標記的有前景解決方案。我們的代碼可在https://github.com/ila-lab/PromptRad獲得。

##### **When Skills Don't Help: A Negative Result on Procedural Knowledge for Tool-Grounded Agents in Offensive Cybersecurity**
2605.20023v1 by Samuel Jacob Chacko, James Hugglestone, Chashi Mahiul Islam, Xiuwen Liu

Agent Skills, structured packages of procedural knowledge loaded into an LLM agent at inference time, are widely reported to improve task pass rates by an average of 16.2~percentage points across diverse domains. Yet the same benchmarks show wide variance, with 16 of 84 tasks suffering negative deltas when Skills are introduced. The community has not yet articulated a clean mechanism for \emph{when} Skills help and when they are merely redundant overhead. We re-analyze a recently published 180-run controlled study of an MCP-grounded autonomous Capture-the-Flag (CTF) agent under four documentation conditions of increasing richness (55, 1{,}478, 1{,}976, and 4{,}147 lines), and show that these conditions correspond almost exactly to a No-Skills, Experiential-Skills, Curated-Skills, and Comprehensive-Skills ablation. In offensive cybersecurity, a domain not deeply covered by existing Skills benchmarks, the marginal benefit of Skills collapses. The spread between the no-Skills and full-Skills conditions is only 8.9~pp ($p = 0.71$, $χ^2$; $p = 0.25$, Cochran--Armitage trend test; five of six pairwise Cohen's $h$ values fall below the $0.2$ small-effect threshold). We argue that the missing variable is \emph{environment-feedback bandwidth}. When an agent's tool layer returns strict, schema-validated, low-latency observations, the environment itself supplies the procedural correction signal that Skills are normally needed to provide. As a result, the marginal benefit of curated Skills diminishes substantially, and, in some cases (e.g., our timing side-channel setting), actively degrades performance. We articulate a falsifiable hypothesis, sketch its design implications for compound AI systems, and will release the reanalysis pipeline to support replication.

摘要：代理技能是結構化的程序知識包，在推理時加載到LLM代理中，據報導在不同領域中平均提高任務通過率16.2個百分點。然而，同樣的基準顯示出廣泛的變異性，在84個任務中有16個在引入技能時出現負增量。社群尚未清楚闡明\emph{何時}技能有幫助，何時它們僅僅是冗餘的開銷。我們重新分析了一項最近發表的180次控制研究，該研究針對一個基於MCP的自主捕旗（CTF）代理，在四種逐漸豐富的文檔條件下（55、1{,}478、1{,}976和4{,}147行），並顯示這些條件幾乎完全對應於無技能、經驗技能、策劃技能和綜合技能的消融。在攻擊性網絡安全這個現有技能基準未深入涵蓋的領域中，技能的邊際效益崩潰。無技能和全技能條件之間的差距僅為8.9個百分點（$p = 0.71$，$χ^2$；$p = 0.25$，Cochran--Armitage趨勢檢驗；六對配對Cohen's $h$值中有五個低於$0.2$的小效應閾值）。我們認為缺失的變量是\emph{環境反饋帶寬}。當代理的工具層返回嚴格的、模式驗證的、低延遲的觀察時，環境本身提供了通常需要技能提供的程序修正信號。因此，策劃技能的邊際效益大幅減少，在某些情況下（例如，我們的計時側信道設置）甚至會主動降低性能。我們闡明了一個可證偽的假設，勾勒出對複合AI系統的設計影響，並將發布重新分析管道以支持複製。

##### **A Case for Agentic Tuning: From Documentation to Action in PostgreSQL**
2605.19988v1 by Hongyu Lin, Mingyu Li, Weichen Zhang, Yihang Lou, Mingjie Xing, Yanjun Wu, Haibo Chen

Documentation has long guided computer system tuning by distilling expert knowledge into per-parameter recommendations. Yet such guides capture only what experts conclude, discarding how they reason. This fundamental gap manifests in three concrete deficiencies: documentation grows stale as software evolves, fails under heterogeneous workloads, and ignores inter-parameter dependencies.
  We propose shifting from static documentation to dynamic action for system tuning. We introduce PerfEvolve, which translates expert tuning methodologies into executable skills that equip LLM-based agents to perform version-consistency verification, workload-specific profiling, and multi-parameter joint optimization. Evaluated on PostgreSQL under TPC-C and TPC-H benchmarks, PerfEvolve outperforms state-of-the-art documentation-driven tuning baselines by up to 35.2%. The tool is available at https://github.com/ISCAS-OSLab/PerfEvolve.

##### **PEEK: Context Map as an Orientation Cache for Long-Context LLM Agents**
2605.19932v1 by Zhuohan Gu, Qizheng Zhang, Omar Khattab, Samuel Madden

Large language model (LLM) agents increasingly operate over long and recurring external contexts, like document corpora and code repositories. Across invocations, existing approaches preserve either the agent's trajectory, passive access to raw material, or task-level strategies. None of them preserves what we argue is most needed for repeated same-context workloads: reusable orientation knowledge (e.g., what the context contains, how it is organized, and which entities, constants, and schemas have historically been useful) about the recurring context itself. We introduce PEEK, a system that caches and maintains this orientation knowledge as a context map: a small, constant-sized artifact in the agent's prompt that gives it a persistent peek into the external context. The map is maintained by a programmable cache policy with three modules: a Distiller that extracts transferable knowledge from inference-time signals, a Cartographer that translates it into structured edits, and a priority-based Evictor that enforces a fixed token budget. On long-context reasoning and information aggregation, PEEK improves over strong baselines by 6.3-34.0% while using 93-145 fewer iterations and incurring 1.7-5.8x lower cost than the state-of-the-art prompt-learning framework, ACE. On context learning, PEEK improves solving rate and rubric accuracy by 6.0-14.0% and 7.8-12.1%, respectively, at 1.4x lower cost than ACE. These gains generalize across LMs and agent architectures, including OpenAI Codex, a production-grade coding agent. Together, these results show that a context map helps long-context LLM agents interact with recurring external contexts more accurately and efficiently.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLM）代理越來越多地在長期和重複的外部上下文中運作，例如文檔語料庫和代碼庫。現有的方法在多次調用中要麼保留代理的軌跡，要麼被動地訪問原材料，或是任務級別的策略。它們都未能保留我們認為對於重複相同上下文工作負載最需要的：可重用的定向知識（例如，上下文包含什麼、如何組織，以及哪些實體、常量和模式在歷史上曾經有用）關於重複的上下文本身。我們介紹了PEEK，一個將這些定向知識緩存並維護為上下文地圖的系統：一個在代理提示中大小固定的小型工件，為其提供持久的外部上下文預覽。該地圖由一個可編程的緩存策略維護，該策略包含三個模塊：一個提煉器，從推理時信號中提取可轉移的知識；一個製圖者，將其轉換為結構化編輯；以及一個基於優先級的驅逐器，強制執行固定的標記預算。在長上下文推理和信息聚合方面，PEEK在使用93-145次更少的迭代且成本比最先進的提示學習框架ACE低1.7-5.8倍的情況下，超越了強基準6.3-34.0%。在上下文學習方面，PEEK的解決率和評分準確度分別提高了6.0-14.0%和7.8-12.1%，成本比ACE低1.4倍。這些增益在各種LM和代理架構中具有普遍性，包括OpenAI Codex，一個生產級的編碼代理。綜合這些結果顯示，上下文地圖幫助長上下文LLM代理更準確和高效地與重複的外部上下文互動。

##### **Synthesis and Evaluation of Long-term History-aware Medical Dialogue**
2605.19766v1 by Hebin Hu, Renke Dai, Ah-Hwee Tan, Yilin Kang

An effective healthcare agent must be able to recall and reason over a patient's longitudinal medical history. However, the absence of datasets with realistic long-term dialogue timelines limits systematic evaluation. Real clinical text is constrained by privacy and ethics, while existing benchmarks focus on isolated interactions, failing to capture cross-session reasoning. We introduce a framework for synthesizing high-quality, long-term medical dialogues with LLMs. Our approach entails a knowledge-guided decomposition into three stages: constructing synthetic patient profiles with diverse disease and complication trajectories, generating multi-turn dialogues per encounter, and integrating them into a coherent longitudinal history dataset, MediLongChat. We establish three benchmark tasks-In-dialogue Reasoning, Cross-dialogue Reasoning, and Synthesis Reasoning-to evaluate the memory capabilities of healthcare agents. ##### **What Really Improves Mathematical Reasoning: Structured Reasoning Signals Beyond Pure Code**
2605.19762v1 by Yuze Zhao, Junpeng Fang, Lu Yu, Zhenya Huang, Kai Zhang, Qing Cui, Qi Liu, Jun Zhou, Enhong Chen

Code has become a standard component of modern foundation language model (LM) training, yet its role beyond programming remains unclear. We revisit the claim that code improves reasoning through controlled pretraining experiments on a 10T-token corpus with fine-grained domain separation. Our findings are threefold. First, when code is restricted to standalone executable programs and Code-NL data are controlled for, code substantially improves programming ability but does not act as a general reasoning enhancer; instead, it competes with knowledge-intensive tasks, especially complex mathematical reasoning. Second, the reasoning gains often attributed to code are better explained by cross-domain structured reasoning traces, such as code-text and math-text mixtures, rather than by executable code alone. Third, increasing the density of structured math-domain samples within a fixed math budget yields substantial gains on difficult mathematical reasoning while largely preserving programming performance, suggesting that cognitive scaffolds offer a targeted way to mitigate cross-domain trade-offs. Finally, routing analyses show that data-composition effects are reflected in expert-activation patterns, providing mechanism-level evidence for competitive and synergistic interactions across domains. Our results clarify which data characteristics transfer across capability dimensions and point to more precise data-centric optimization strategies.
