##### **Discoverable Agent Knowledge -- A Formal Framework for Agentic KG Affordances (Extended Version)**
2605.19186v1 by Terry R. Payne, Valentina Tamma, Enrico Daga

Two decades ago, the Semantic Web Services community was asked how agents with different ontological commitments could discover, compose, and invoke web services coherently. The response was OWL-S and WSMO: formally grounded capability descriptions specifying what a service could do, what the agent must already know for invocation to be epistemically sound, and how ontological mismatches could be formally bridged. Current Knowledge Graph (KG) metadata standards such as VoID and DCAT describe what a KG contains yet say nothing about what a specific agent can prove from it, what closure assumptions govern empty results, or whether the agent's task vocabulary is grounded in the schema. Furthermore, in deployed KGs the governing schema DL and the operative entailment regime can diverge: an epistemic failure mode invisible to current metadata. We revisit and extend these insights for the KG setting with a four-dimensional formal framework from which we derive the Agentic Affordance Profile (AAP): a semantic layer above VoID and DCAT enabling principled KG selection, composition, and failure diagnosis at agent planning time. A five-point research agenda identifies the formal, computational, and engineering work needed to realise AAP-based affordance matching at scale.

摘要：二十年前，語意網服務社群被問及，具有不同本體承諾的代理人如何能夠一致地發現、組合和調用網路服務。回應是 OWL-S 和 WSMO：這些是正式基礎的能力描述，指定服務可以做什麼，代理人必須已經知道什麼以使調用在認識論上是合理的，以及如何正式橋接本體不匹配。目前的知識圖譜（KG）元數據標準，如 VoID 和 DCAT，描述了 KG 內容，但對於特定代理人能從中證明什麼、空結果的閉合假設如何運作，或代理人的任務詞彙是否基於架構，則沒有說明。此外，在已部署的 KG 中，治理架構的描述邏輯（DL）和操作推理體系可能會有所不同：這是一種對當前元數據不可見的認識論失敗模式。我們重新檢視並擴展這些見解，針對 KG 設定提出一個四維的正式框架，從中衍生出代理可供性概況（AAP）：這是一個位於 VoID 和 DCAT 之上的語意層，能夠在代理規劃時實現原則性的 KG 選擇、組合和失敗診斷。一個五點研究議程確定了實現基於 AAP 的可供性匹配所需的正式、計算和工程工作。

##### **Bridge: Retrieval-Augmented Spatiotemporal Modeling for Urban Delivery Demand**
2605.19172v1 by Yihong Tang, Tong Nie, Junlin He, Qianjun Huang, Dingyi Zhuang, Lijun Sun

Forecasting urban delivery demand becomes substantially more challenging when newly added service regions lack historical records. Existing spatiotemporal forecasters effectively model spatial dependence once sufficient node histories are available. Still, they remain parametric and therefore struggle to recover short-term operational dynamics in cold-start regions. Geospatial embeddings help identify where a region is and what function it serves, yet they do not directly reveal how a similar region behaves under a comparable temporal context. We propose Bridge, a retrieval-augmented spatiotemporal graph framework that combines an inductive contextual graph backbone with a time-aware memory of region-time windows. For each target region, Bridge retrieves future demand patterns from the memory using both regional context and recent dynamics, and refines the backbone forecast through a gated fusion mechanism. To align retrieval with forecasting utility, we further train the retriever with a future-aware objective that favors entries whose future trajectories best match the target. Experiments on four real-world delivery datasets show that Bridge consistently improves over competitive spatiotemporal baselines in both within-city cold-start and cross-city transfer with partial observations. The results show that retrieval augmentation provides a useful operational memory for cold-start urban demand forecasting when parametric graph generalization alone is insufficient.

摘要：預測城市配送需求在新增服務區域缺乏歷史記錄時變得相當具有挑戰性。現有的時空預測模型在有足夠的節點歷史記錄時能有效地建模空間依賴性。儘管如此，它們仍然是參數化的，因此在冷啟動區域中難以恢復短期操作動態。地理空間嵌入有助於識別一個區域的位置及其所服務的功能，但它們並未直接揭示類似區域在可比較的時間背景下的行為。我們提出了Bridge，一個檢索增強的時空圖框架，結合了歸納上下文圖的骨幹和對區域-時間窗口的時間感知記憶。對於每個目標區域，Bridge利用區域上下文和近期動態從記憶中檢索未來需求模式，並通過門控融合機制來細化骨幹預測。為了使檢索與預測效用對齊，我們進一步以未來感知的目標訓練檢索器，偏好那些未來軌跡與目標最匹配的條目。在四個真實世界的配送數據集上的實驗顯示，Bridge在城市內冷啟動和跨城市轉移的部分觀察中，始終優於競爭性的時空基準。結果顯示，檢索增強為冷啟動城市需求預測提供了一個有用的操作記憶，當參數化圖的泛化能力不足時。

##### **Catching a Moving Subspace: Low-Rank Bandits Beyond Stationarity**
2605.20269v1 by Hamed Khosravi, Xiaoming Huo

Many bandit deployments (recommendation, clinical dosing, ad targeting) share two facts prior work handles only in isolation: rewards live on a low-dimensional latent subspace, and that subspace drifts. Stationary low-rank bandits exploit rank but break under subspace change; non-stationary linear bandits adapt to drift but pay ambient rate $\widetilde{O}(d\sqrt{T})$. We study piecewise-stationary low-rank linear contextual bandits with scalar feedback: $θ_t = B_k^\star w_t$ with rank-$r$ factor $B_k^\star\in\mathbb{R}^{d\times r}$ constant within each of $K$ unknown segments and able to shift at boundaries. Our results are tight along three axes. (i) Identification boundary. With single-play scalar rewards, the moving subspace is recoverable through quadratic functionals of rewards iff three probe-side conditions hold: known noise variance, bounded state-noise coupling, and full-dimensional probe support. Each is necessary in the unrestricted-second-moment problem, and jointly they are sufficient, characterizing the boundary of the solvable region. (ii) Algorithm and dynamic regret. SPSC interleaves isotropic probes with windowed projected ridge-UCB exploitation inside the learned $r$-dimensional subspace; a CUSUM-style variant discovers segment boundaries online. The costed dynamic regret is $\widetilde{O}(r\sqrt{T})+\widetilde{O}(T^{2/3})+O(W\,V_{\mathrm{in}})$, replacing the ambient $d\sqrt{T}$ rate with the intrinsic rank. (iii) Empirics. On eleven benchmarks spanning synthetic, UCI/MovieLens, semi-synthetic clinical, and ZOZOTOWN production-log data, SPSC outperforms non-stationary and low-rank baselines whenever $d-r\gtrsim T^{1/6}$, matching the analytical crossover. To our knowledge, this is the first work to characterize the identification boundary and attain the intrinsic-rank dynamic-regret rate in this setting.

摘要：許多強盜部署（推薦、臨床劑量、廣告定位）共享兩個事實，之前的工作僅在孤立中處理：獎勵位於低維潛在子空間中，且該子空間會漂移。靜態低秩強盜利用秩但在子空間變化時失效；非靜態線性強盜適應漂移但需支付環境速率 $\widetilde{O}(d\sqrt{T})$。我們研究具有標量反饋的分段靜態低秩線性上下文強盜：$θ_t = B_k^\star w_t$，其中秩為$r$的因子 $B_k^\star\in\mathbb{R}^{d\times r}$ 在$K$個未知段內保持不變，並能在邊界處變化。我們的結果在三個軸上是緊湊的。（i）識別邊界。對於單次遊玩標量獎勵，移動子空間可以通過獎勵的二次泛函來恢復，當且僅當三個探測側條件成立：已知噪聲方差、有界狀態-噪聲耦合，以及全維度探測支持。每一條件在不受限的二次矩問題中都是必要的，並且它們共同足以表徵可解區域的邊界。（ii）算法和動態遺憾。SPSC 將各向同性探測與在學習到的$r$維子空間內的窗口化投影脊-UCB 利用交錯；一種CUSUM風格的變體在線發現段邊界。計算的動態遺憾為 $\widetilde{O}(r\sqrt{T})+\widetilde{O}(T^{2/3})+O(W\,V_{\mathrm{in}})$，用內在秩替換了環境 $d\sqrt{T}$ 的速率。（iii）實證。在涵蓋合成、UCI/MovieLens、半合成臨床和 ZOZOTOWN 生產日誌數據的十一個基準上，當 $d-r\gtrsim T^{1/6}$ 時，SPSC 超越了非靜態和低秩基準，與分析交叉點相匹配。據我們所知，這是第一項在此設置中表徵識別邊界並達到內在秩動態遺憾速率的工作。

##### **GRASP: Deterministic argument ranking in interaction graphs**
2605.19141v1 by Diganta Misra, Antonio Orvieto, Rediet Abebe, Volkan Cevher

Large language models are increasingly deployed as automated judges to evaluate the strength of arguments. As this role expands, their legitimacy depends on consistency, transparency, and the ability to separate argumentative structure from rhetorical appeal. However, we show that holistic judging - a common LLM-as-a-Judge practice where a model provides a global verdict on a debate - suffers from substantial inter-model disagreement. We argue that this instability arises from collapsing a debate's complex interaction structure into a single opaque score. To address this, we propose GRASP (Gradual Ranking with Attacks and Support Propagation), a deterministic framework that aggregates stable local interaction judgments into a global ranking via a convergent attack--defense propagation operator. We show that local interaction judgments are more reproducible than holistic rankings in LLM-as-a-Judge evaluations, allowing GRASP to produce more consistent global rankings. We further show that GRASP scores do not correlate with human "convincingness" labels, highlighting a vital sociotechnical distinction: GRASP does not measure persuasion, factuality, or rhetorical appeal, but structural sufficiency - a defense-aware notion of argument robustness over the explicit interaction graph. Overall, GRASP offers a transparent and auditable alternative to holistic LLM judging.

摘要：大型語言模型越來越多地被用作自動評判者，以評估論點的強度。隨著這一角色的擴展，它們的合法性依賴於一致性、透明度以及將論證結構與修辭吸引力分開的能力。 然而，我們顯示出整體評判——一種常見的 LLM 作為評判者的做法，其中模型對辯論提供全球判決——存在顯著的模型間不一致。我們認為，這種不穩定性源於將辯論的複雜互動結構簡化為單一不透明的分數。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了 GRASP（逐步排名與攻擊和支持傳播），這是一個確定性的框架，通過收斂的攻擊-防禦傳播運算符將穩定的局部互動判斷聚合成全球排名。我們顯示，在 LLM 作為評判者的評估中，局部互動判斷比整體排名更具可重現性，使 GRASP 能夠產生更一致的全球排名。我們進一步顯示，GRASP 分數與人類的「說服力」標籤不相關，突顯出一個重要的社會技術區別：GRASP 不測量說服力、事實性或修辭吸引力，而是結構充分性——一種對明確互動圖的防禦意識的論證穩健性概念。總的來說，GRASP 提供了一種透明且可審計的替代方案，以取代整體 LLM 評判。

##### **Learning to Hand Off: Provably Convergent Workflow Learning under Interface Constraints**
2605.19140v1 by Jiayu Li, Enpei Zhang, Dawei Zhou, Elynn Chen, Yujun Yan

We study workflow learning in a setting where specialized agents hand off control through a shared artifact, each agent observes only a local function of that artifact and its own private state, and no centralized learner accesses joint trajectories -- the operating regime of multi-agent LLM pipelines that span organizational, vendor, or trust boundaries. We formalize this regime as an interface-constrained semi-Markov decision process (IC-SMDP), whose decision epochs occur at handoff times, and design IC-$Q$, an asynchronous decentralized $Q$-learning algorithm in which cross-agent coordination at every handoff is exactly one scalar. Our main result is a finite-sample bound for neural IC-$Q$ that decomposes into three independently controllable error sources: neural function-approximation error, interface representation gap, and a mixing-time residual, under the random option-duration discount. Establishing this bound requires lifting the approximate information state (AIS) framework from single-agent primitive-step MDPs to multi-agent SMDPs and controlling Markovian noise under random duration, neither of which has been done in prior work. To our knowledge this is the first finite-sample guarantee for neural $Q$-learning under decentralized partial observability. Four experiments: a controlled synthetic IC-SMDP that validates the bound term-by-term, multi-LLM mathematical reasoning, multi-agent routing, and multi-agent CPU programming, show that IC-$Q$ matches a centralized oracle without any agent observing joint trajectories, with each of the three error sources scaling along its corresponding axis as the bound predicts.

摘要：我們研究在一個專門代理透過共享工件交接控制的環境中的工作流程學習，每個代理僅觀察該工件的局部功能及其自身的私有狀態，且沒有集中式學習者訪問聯合軌跡——這是跨越組織、供應商或信任邊界的多代理 LLM 管道的操作模式。我們將這一模式形式化為一種接口約束的半馬爾可夫決策過程（IC-SMDP），其決策時刻發生在交接時，並設計了 IC-$Q$，這是一種異步去中心化的 $Q$-學習算法，其中每次交接時的跨代理協調正好是一個標量。我們的主要結果是對神經 IC-$Q$ 的有限樣本界限，該界限分解為三個獨立可控的誤差來源：神經函數近似誤差、接口表示差距，以及隨機選項持續折扣下的混合時間殘差。建立這一界限需要將近似信息狀態（AIS）框架從單代理原始步驟 MDP 提升到多代理 SMDP，並在隨機持續時間下控制馬爾可夫噪聲，這兩者在之前的工作中都未曾實現。據我們所知，這是首個在去中心化部分可觀察性下對神經 $Q$-學習的有限樣本保證。四個實驗：一個受控的合成 IC-SMDP 驗證了界限逐項的正確性，多 LLM 數學推理，多代理路由，以及多代理 CPU 編程，顯示 IC-$Q$ 在沒有任何代理觀察聯合軌跡的情況下匹配了一個集中式的神諭，且三個誤差來源各自在其對應的軸上隨著界限的預測而擴展。

##### **Chronicle: A Multimodal Foundation Model for Joint Language and Time Series Understanding**
2605.20268v1 by Paul Quinlan, Jeremy Levasseur, Qingguo Li, Xiaodan Zhu

Real-world time series come with text: metadata, descriptions, news, reports. Yet time series foundation models process numerical sequences in isolation, and the multimodal text-and-time-series models that attempt to bridge the two all adapt a pretrained language model post hoc, inheriting representations shaped without ever seeing temporal data. These models are also evaluated almost exclusively against other multimodal baselines, not against the strongest unimodal foundation models in either domain, leaving open whether joint training is needed at all. We present Chronicle, a compact 324M-parameter decoder-only transformer trained from scratch on natural language and time series within a single unified architecture. Both modalities share the same transformer blocks, attention mechanism, and residual stream; the bulk of pretraining uses unimodal batches so cross-modal capability emerges purely from shared parameters, with a short alignment stage that interleaves the two. To our knowledge, Chronicle is the first model jointly pretrained on text and time series from scratch, and the first multimodal model evaluated against dedicated foundation models in both domains. It matches Gemma-3-270M-PT on 19 NLU tasks, sets a new bar for frozen-embedding time series classification on 24 UCR/UEA datasets, and produces multimodal forecasts on Time-MMD that beat every supervised fusion baseline, all from a single backbone.

摘要：現實世界的時間序列伴隨著文本：元數據、描述、新聞、報告。然而，時間序列基礎模型在孤立中處理數值序列，而試圖橋接兩者的多模態文本與時間序列模型都在事後調整預訓練的語言模型，繼承了在未曾接觸時間數據的情況下形成的表示。這些模型幾乎完全是針對其他多模態基準進行評估，而不是針對任何領域中最強的單模態基礎模型，這使得聯合訓練是否真的必要仍然懸而未決。我們提出了Chronicle，一個緊湊的324M參數的僅解碼器Transformer，從零開始在自然語言和時間序列上進行訓練，並在單一統一架構內運作。兩種模態共享相同的Transformer塊、注意力機制和殘差流；大部分的預訓練使用單模態批次，因此跨模態能力純粹來自共享參數，並有一個短暫的對齊階段將兩者交錯在一起。據我們所知，Chronicle是第一個從零開始在文本和時間序列上進行聯合預訓練的模型，也是第一個在兩個領域中針對專用基礎模型進行評估的多模態模型。它在19個NLU任務上與Gemma-3-270M-PT匹配，為24個UCR/UEA數據集上的凍結嵌入時間序列分類設立了新的標準，並在Time-MMD上產生的多模態預測超越了每個監督融合基準，所有這些都來自單一的骨幹。

##### **FAGER: Factually Grounded Evaluation and Refinement of Text-to-Image Models**
2605.19111v1 by Youngsun Lim, Cusuh Ham, Pin-Yu Chen, Deepti Ghadiyaram

Existing text-to-image (T2I) evaluation metrics mainly assess whether generated images align with information explicitly stated in the prompt, but often fail to capture factual requirements that are implicit, externally grounded, or identity-defining. As a result, they are not well suited for evaluating factual correctness in prompts involving scientific knowledge, historical facts, products, or culture-specific concepts. We propose FActually Grounded Evaluation and Refinement (FAGER), an agentic framework that evaluates whether generated images correctly reflect visually verifiable facts grounded in or implied by the prompt, while also providing actionable feedback for improvement. FAGER first constructs a structured factual rubric by combining LLM-based fact proposal with reference-guided visual fact extraction and verification, then converts the rubric into question-answer pairs for VLM-based evaluation. To validate FAGER as a factuality metric, we introduce a Factual A/B test, which measures whether a metric prefers factual reference images over corresponding generated images. Across five datasets spanning science, history, products, culture, and knowledge-intensive concepts, FAGER consistently outperforms prior metrics on this test. We further show that FAGER can be used to refine T2I outputs in a fully training-free manner, yielding substantial factuality gains across datasets.

摘要：現有的文本到圖像 (T2I) 評估指標主要評估生成的圖像是否與提示中明確陳述的信息一致，但往往無法捕捉隱含的、外部基礎的或身份定義的事實要求。因此，它們不太適合評估涉及科學知識、歷史事實、產品或文化特定概念的提示中的事實正確性。我們提出了實際基礎評估與改進 (FAGER)，這是一個代理框架，用於評估生成的圖像是否正確反映基於提示的可視驗證事實，並提供可行的改進反饋。FAGER 首先通過結合基於 LLM 的事實提議與參考引導的視覺事實提取和驗證來構建結構化的事實標準，然後將該標準轉換為問題-答案對以進行基於 VLM 的評估。為了驗證 FAGER 作為事實性指標的有效性，我們引入了一個事實 A/B 測試，該測試測量指標是否偏好事實參考圖像而非相應的生成圖像。在涵蓋科學、歷史、產品、文化和知識密集型概念的五個數據集上，FAGER 在這一測試中始終優於之前的指標。我們進一步表明，FAGER 可以以完全無需訓練的方式來改進 T2I 輸出，並在各數據集上實現顯著的事實性提升。

##### **Counterfactual Likelihood Tests for Indirect Influence in Private Reasoning Channels**
2605.19092v1 by Alexander Boesgaard Lorup

Reasoning systems increasingly separate intermediate computation into private and public channels, creating evaluation cases that look similar in transcripts: independent co-derivation, direct access to private content, and indirect influence through public communication. This paper presents a counterfactual likelihood test for measuring influence between private reasoning channels. The method replaces an upstream private block with a length-matched donor block, holds the public token sequence and downstream target fixed, and measures the downstream target's negative-log-likelihood shift. On a 7B role-channel reasoning model used for validation, textual probes are unreliable: raw n-gram overlap overstates leakage, corrected overlap remains noisy, and canary reproduction reports no discrimination. Counterfactual likelihood separates unmasked and masked conditions, while length matching controls a RoPE positional confound. In the hardened masked validation, reverse B-to-A influence is near zero, while A-to-B influence persists through public-speech hidden states. A multi-checkpoint validation across three checkpoints, five seeds, and 13,734 valid directional contrasts replicates this asymmetry. A graph-separation control that blocks private-to-public carrier edges produces bit-identical natural and counterfactual scores across all 13,734 control evaluations, identifying the tested public-channel pathway as the complete carrier of the measured counterfactual signal under the implemented role-visibility mask. The results show that private-channel evaluation should report direct and indirect influence separately, and that counterfactual likelihood probes provide a practical default for measuring these boundaries.

摘要：推理系統越來越多地將中間計算分為私有和公有通道，創造出在記錄中看起來相似的評估案例：獨立共同推導、對私有內容的直接訪問，以及通過公共溝通的間接影響。本文提出了一種反事實可能性測試，用於測量私有推理通道之間的影響。該方法用一個長度匹配的捐贈塊替換上游的私有塊，保持公共令牌序列和下游目標不變，並測量下游目標的負對數可能性變化。在用於驗證的7B角色通道推理模型上，文本探針不可靠：原始n-gram重疊高估了洩漏，修正後的重疊仍然嘈雜，且金絲雀重現報告無法區分。反事實可能性將未掩碼和掩碼條件分開，而長度匹配則控制了RoPE位置混淆。在強化的掩碼驗證中，反向B到A的影響接近於零，而A到B的影響則通過公共演講的隱藏狀態持續存在。跨越三個檢查點、五個種子和13,734個有效方向對比的多檢查點驗證複製了這種不對稱性。一個阻止私有到公共承載邊緣的圖形分離控制在所有13,734個控制評估中產生了位元相同的自然和反事實分數，確定了經過實施的角色可見性掩碼下測量的反事實信號的完整承載通道。結果顯示，私有通道評估應分別報告直接和間接影響，並且反事實可能性探針提供了一個實用的默認方法來測量這些邊界。

##### **Toward an AI-Powered Computational Testbed for Workforce Policy**
2605.19064v1 by Sumer S. Vaid, Ashley V. Whillans

Workforce transformations are difficult to forecast and costly to mismanage. In particular, the integration of artificial intelligence into knowledge work currently affects a substantial share of the global workforce, yet this transition proceeds without tools to forecast how individual employees will respond psychologically and behaviorally. We combine recent advances in LLM-powered generative agents with foundational management science and organizational behavior research to propose dynamic employee agents. Among consenting populations, these agents can be seeded with HR records, validated psychometric measures, and digital activity data to simulate employees' cognitive, emotional, and behavioral trajectories across successive workdays during planned organizational changes. In this article, we detail the computational architecture required to construct this simulation platform and define the privacy, accuracy, and representativeness safeguards necessary for responsible deployment. We argue that establishing this prospective forecasting infrastructure is a critical technical requirement for managing the current global workforce realignment around AI.

摘要：勞動力轉型難以預測，且錯誤管理的成本高昂。<lb/>特別是，人工智慧在知識工作中的整合目前影響著全球勞動力的相當一部分，但這一過渡卻在缺乏預測個別員工心理和行為反應的工具的情況下進行。<lb/>我們結合了最近在大型語言模型驅動的生成代理方面的進展與基礎管理科學和組織行為研究，提出了動態員工代理。<lb/>在同意的群體中，這些代理可以利用人力資源記錄、經過驗證的心理測量指標和數位活動數據來模擬員工在計劃中的組織變革期間，隨著工作日的推移，認知、情感和行為的軌跡。<lb/>在本文中，我們詳細說明了構建這一模擬平台所需的計算架構，並定義了負責任部署所需的隱私、準確性和代表性保障措施。<lb/>我們主張，建立這一前瞻性預測基礎設施是管理當前全球勞動力因人工智慧而重新調整的關鍵技術要求。

##### **ESI-Bench: Towards Embodied Spatial Intelligence that Closes the Perception-Action Loop**
2605.18746v1 by Yining Hong, Jiageng Liu, Han Yin, Manling Li, Leonidas Guibas, Li Fei-Fei, Jiajun Wu, Yejin Choi

Spatial intelligence unfolds through a perception-action loop: agents act to acquire observations, and reason about how observations vary as a function of action. Rather than passively processing what is seen, they actively uncover what is unseen - occluded structure, dynamics, containment, and functionality that cannot be resolved from passive sensing alone. We move beyond prior formulations of spatial intelligence that assume oracle observations by recasting the observer as an actor. We introduce ESI-BENCH, a comprehensive benchmark for embodied spatial intelligence spanning 10 task categories and 29 subcategories built on OmniGibson, grounded in Spelke's core knowledge systems. Agents must decide what abilities to deploy - perception, locomotion, and manipulation - and how to sequence them to actively accumulate task-relevant evidence. We conduct extensive experiments on state-of-the-art MLLMs and find that active exploration substantially outperforms passive counterparts, with agents spontaneously discovering emergent spatial strategies without explicit instructions, while random multi-view often adds noise rather than signal despite consuming far more images. Most failures stem not from weak perception but from action blindness: poor action choices lead to poor observations, which in turn drive cascading errors. While explicit 3D grounding stabilizes reasoning on depth-sensitive tasks, imperfect 3D representation proves more harmful than 2D baselines by distorting spatial relations. Human studies further reveal that unlike humans who seek falsifying viewpoints and revise beliefs under contradiction, models commit prematurely with high confidence regardless of evidence quality, exposing a metacognitive gap that neither better perception nor more embodied interaction alone can close.

摘要：空間智能通過感知-行動循環展開：代理人行動以獲取觀察，並推理觀察如何隨著行動而變化。它們不僅被動處理所見之物，而是主動揭示那些未被看到的東西——被遮蔽的結構、動態、包含性和功能，這些是僅靠被動感知無法解析的。我們超越了以往假設神諭觀察的空間智能表述，將觀察者重新塑造為行動者。我們介紹ESI-BENCH，一個全面的體現空間智能的基準，涵蓋10個任務類別和29個子類別，基於OmniGibson，根植於Spelke的核心知識系統。代理人必須決定部署哪些能力——感知、運動和操作——以及如何對它們進行排序，以主動積累與任務相關的證據。我們對最先進的MLLMs進行了廣泛實驗，發現主動探索明顯優於被動對應物，代理人自發地發現新興的空間策略，而無需明確指示，儘管隨機多視角通常會增加噪音而非信號，卻消耗了更多的圖像。大多數失敗並非來自於感知薄弱，而是源於行動盲點：糟糕的行動選擇導致糟糕的觀察，進而驅動連鎖錯誤。雖然明確的3D基礎穩定了對深度敏感任務的推理，但不完美的3D表徵比2D基準更具危害性，因為它扭曲了空間關係。人類研究進一步揭示，與尋求反駁觀點並在矛盾中修正信念的人類不同，模型則在證據質量無關的情況下過早地以高信心做出決策，暴露出一個元認知差距，僅靠更好的感知或更多的體現互動無法彌補。

##### **Distilling Tabular Foundation Models for Structured Health Data**
2605.18702v1 by Aditya Tanna, Nassim Bouarour, Mohamed Bouadi, Vinay Kumar Sankarapu, Pratinav Seth

Tabular foundation models (TFMs) achieve strong performance on health datasets, but their inference cost and infrastructure requirements limit practical use. We study whether their predictive behavior can be transferred to lightweight tabular models through knowledge distillation. Since in-context TFMs condition on the training set at inference time, naive distillation can introduce context leakage; we address this with stratified out-of-fold teacher labeling. Across $19$ healthcare datasets, $6$ TFM teachers, $4$ student families, and several multi-teacher ensembles, we find that distilled students retain at least $90\%$ of teacher AUC, outperforming teachers in some cases, while running at least $26\times$ faster on CPU and preserving calibration and fairness critical for health applications. Moreover, multi-teacher averaging does not consistently improve over the best single teacher. Leakage-aware distillation is thus a viable route for bringing TFM-quality predictions into inference-constrained health settings.

摘要：表格基礎模型（TFMs）在健康數據集上表現出色，但其推斷成本和基礎設施需求限制了實際應用。我們研究了它們的預測行為是否可以通過知識蒸餾轉移到輕量級表格模型。由於上下文TFMs在推斷時依賴於訓練集，天真的蒸餾可能會引入上下文洩漏；我們通過分層的外部教師標記來解決這個問題。在$19$個醫療數據集中，$6$個TFM教師，$4$個學生家族，以及幾個多教師集成中，我們發現蒸餾後的學生至少保留了$90\%$的教師AUC，在某些情況下超越教師，同時在CPU上運行速度至少快$26\times$，並保持對健康應用至關重要的校準和公平性。此外，多教師平均並不總是優於最佳單一教師。因此，意識到洩漏的蒸餾是一條可行的路徑，可以將TFM質量的預測引入受限推斷的健康環境中。

##### **COOPO: Cyclic Offline-Online Policy Optimization Algorithm**
2605.18675v1 by Qisai Liu, Zhanhong Jiang, Joshua Russell Waite, Aditya Balu, Cody Fleming, Soumik Sarkar

Offline reinforcement learning struggles with distributional shift and constrained performance due to static dataset limitations, while online RL demands prohibitive environment interactions. The recent advent of hybrid offline-to-online methods bridges these domains but suffers from distribution drift during transitions and catastrophic forgetting of offline knowledge. We introduce COOPO (Cyclic Offline-Online Policy Optimization), a generalized framework that repeatedly cycles between constrained offline training and online fine-tuning. Each cycle first anchors the policy to the dataset via KL-regularized advantage-weighted offline updates to minimize distributional shift and then fine-tunes it online using any policy optimization for stable exploration. Crucially, periodically returning to offline training eliminates forgetting and drift while maximizing dataset reuse. The cyclic behavior also helps reduce the online environment interactions. Theoretically, COOPO achieves better online sample efficiency, surpassing pure online RL, with guaranteed monotonic improvement under standard coverage assumptions. Extensive D4RL benchmarks demonstrate COOPO reduces online interactions versus state-of-the-art hybrids while improving final returns, maintaining robustness across diverse offline algorithms and online optimizers. This looped synergy sets new efficiency and performance standards for adaptive RL.

摘要：離線強化學習因靜態數據集的限制而面臨分佈轉移和性能受限的挑戰，而在線強化學習則需要大量的環境互動。最近出現的混合離線到在線方法橋接了這些領域，但在過渡期間遭遇分佈漂移和離線知識的災難性遺忘。我們引入了 COOPO（循環離線-在線策略優化），這是一個通用框架，重複循環於受限的離線訓練和在線微調之間。每個循環首先通過 KL 正則化的優勢加權離線更新將策略固定於數據集，以最小化分佈轉移，然後使用任何策略優化方法在線微調，以實現穩定的探索。關鍵是，定期返回離線訓練可消除遺忘和漂移，同時最大化數據集的重用。循環行為還有助於減少在線環境互動。在理論上，COOPO 實現了更好的在線樣本效率，超越純在線強化學習，並在標準覆蓋假設下保證單調改進。廣泛的 D4RL 基準測試顯示，COOPO 減少了與最先進混合方法相比的在線互動，同時改善了最終回報，並在多樣的離線算法和在線優化器中保持穩健性。這種循環協同為自適應強化學習設立了新的效率和性能標準。

##### **GIM: Evaluating models via tasks that integrate multiple cognitive domains**
2605.18663v1 by Rohit Patel, Alexandre Rezende, Steven McClain

As LLM benchmarks saturate, the evaluation community has pursued two strategies to increase difficulty: escalating knowledge demands (GPQA, HLE) or removing knowledge entirely in favor of abstract reasoning (ARC-AGI). The first conflates memorization with capability; the second divorces reasoning from the practical contexts in which it matters. We take a different approach. The Grounded Integration Measure (GIM) is a benchmark of 820 original problems (615 public, 205 private) where difficulty comes from integration; individual problems require coordinating multiple cognitive operations (constraint satisfaction, state tracking, epistemic vigilance, audience calibration) over broadly accessible knowledge, so that reasoning stays grounded in realistic tasks without being gated on specialized expertise. Each problem is an original expert-authored composition, majority with rubric-decomposed scoring (median 6 independently judged criteria). A balanced public--private split provides built-in contamination diagnostic. We calibrate a continuous response 2-parameter logistic (2PL) IRT model over >200k prompt-response pairs across 28 models, producing robust ability estimates that correctly order test-configurations even when raw accuracy is distorted by errors or missing data, addressing a common challenge in benchmark reporting. Using this framework, we present a comprehensive leaderboard spanning 22 models and 47 test-configurations (unique model, thinking-level pairs), and conduct what is to our knowledge the most extensive published study of how test-time compute trades off against model capability on a fixed benchmark: 11 models swept across 35 test-configurations. We observe that within-family configuration choices, such as thinking budget and quantization, matter as much as model selection. We release the evaluation framework, calibrated IRT parameters, and all public problems.

摘要：隨著大型語言模型（LLM）基準測試的飽和，評估社群採取了兩種策略來提高難度：增加知識需求（GPQA、HLE）或完全移除知識以偏向抽象推理（ARC-AGI）。第一種方法將記憶與能力混為一談；第二種方法則將推理與其重要的實際情境割裂。我們採取不同的方法。基於整合測量（GIM）是一個包含820個原創問題（615個公開，205個私有）的基準，難度來自於整合；每個問題需要協調多個認知操作（約束滿足、狀態追蹤、認知警覺、受眾校準），並基於廣泛可獲得的知識，使得推理保持在現實任務中，而不受限於專業知識。每個問題都是原創的專家撰寫的作品，大多數問題都使用了分解評分的標準（中位數6個獨立評判標準）。平衡的公開與私有分配提供了內建的污染診斷。我們在超過20萬個提示-回應對中，對28個模型進行了連續響應的2參數邏輯（2PL）IRT模型的校準，產生了穩健的能力估計，即使在原始準確度因錯誤或缺失數據而失真時，也能正確排序測試配置，解決了基準報告中的一個常見挑戰。利用這一框架，我們呈現了一個涵蓋22個模型和47個測試配置（獨特模型、思維層級對）的綜合排行榜，並進行了我們所知的最廣泛的已發表研究，探討了測試時計算如何與固定基準上的模型能力進行權衡：11個模型掃描了35個測試配置。我們觀察到，在同一家族的配置選擇中，如思維預算和量化，與模型選擇一樣重要。我們發布了評估框架、校準的IRT參數以及所有公開問題。

##### **KairosHope: A Next-Generation Time-Series Foundation Model for Specialized Classification via Dual-Memory Architecture**
2605.18657v1 by Luis Balderas, José Alberto Rodríguez, Miguel Lastra, Antonio Arauzo-Azofra, José M. Benítez

Time Series Foundation Models (TSFMs) have demonstrated notable success in general-purpose forecasting tasks; however, their adaptation to specialized classification problems remains constrained by the computational bottleneck of standard attention and the systematic omission of classical statistical knowledge. This technical report introduces KairosHope, a next-generation TSFM designed to reconcile massive generalization with analytical precision in classification tasks. The core of the proposal is the HOPE block, an architecture that replaces quadratic attention with a dual-memory system: Titans modules for dynamic short-term retention and a Continuum Memory System (CMS) for the abstraction of long-term historical context. To enrich the inductive bias, a Hybrid Decision Head is introduced, which fuses deep latent representations with deterministic statistical features extracted via tsfeatures package. KairosHope undergoes self-supervised pre-training on the massive Monash archive, combining Masked Time Series Modeling (MTSM) and contrastive learning (InfoNCE). Its subsequent adaptation to the UCR benchmark datasets is conducted through a rigorous Linear Probing and Full Fine-Tuning (LP-FT) protocol to prevent catastrophic forgetting. Empirical results demonstrate superior performance in domains characterized by strict temporal causality such as HAR or Sensor data. Consequently, KairosHope establishes a robust and efficient framework for the adaptation of foundation models to time series analysis.

摘要：時間序列基礎模型（TSFM）在通用預測任務中已顯示出顯著的成功；然而，它們在專門分類問題上的適應仍受到標準注意力的計算瓶頸和系統性省略傳統統計知識的限制。這份技術報告介紹了KairosHope，一種下一代TSFM，旨在調和大規模泛化與分類任務中的分析精確性。該提案的核心是HOPE區塊，一種用雙重記憶系統取代二次注意力的架構：Titans模塊用於動態短期保留，而連續記憶系統（CMS）則用於長期歷史上下文的抽象。為了豐富歸納偏差，引入了一個混合決策頭，該頭將深度潛在表示與通過tsfeatures套件提取的確定性統計特徵融合在一起。KairosHope在龐大的Monash檔案庫上進行自我監督的預訓練，結合了遮蔽時間序列建模（MTSM）和對比學習（InfoNCE）。隨後，它對UCR基準數據集的適應是通過嚴格的線性探測和完全微調（LP-FT）協議進行的，以防止災難性遺忘。實證結果顯示，在如HAR或傳感器數據等以嚴格時間因果關係為特徵的領域中，表現優越。因此，KairosHope建立了一個穩健且高效的框架，以將基礎模型適應於時間序列分析。

##### **Position: Weight Space Should Be a First-Class Generative AI Modality**
2605.18632v1 by Zhangyang Wang, Peihao Wang, Kai Wang

Neural network checkpoints have quietly become a large-scale data resource: millions of trained weight vectors now exist, each encoding task-, domain-, and architecture-specific knowledge. This position paper argues that model checkpoints should be treated as a first-class data modality, and that generative modeling in weight space should be standardized as a core machine learning primitive. Recent advances demonstrate that neural weights can be synthesized on demand, often matching fine-tuning performance while reducing adaptation cost by orders of magnitude. We contend that these results reflect an underlying structural fact: high-performing models occupy low-dimensional, highly structured regions of weight space shaped by symmetry, flatness, modularity, and shared subspaces. Building on this view, we organize existing methods into a five-stage pipeline, survey applications where the approach is already practical, and clarify current limits: adapter-scale and conditional generation are advancing rapidly, while unrestricted frontier-scale checkpoint synthesis remains open. Our goal is to shift the community's default mindset from optimizing models per task to sampling models from learned weight distributions, accelerating toward an era in which AI systems routinely improve or create other AI systems.

摘要：神經網絡檢查點已悄然成為一種大規模數據資源：目前存在數百萬個訓練過的權重向量，每個向量都編碼了特定於任務、領域和架構的知識。這篇立場論文主張，模型檢查點應被視為一種一流的數據模式，並且在權重空間中的生成建模應標準化為核心機器學習原語。最近的進展顯示，神經權重可以按需合成，通常在減少適應成本的同時，匹配微調性能。我們認為這些結果反映了一個潛在的結構事實：高性能模型佔據了由對稱性、平坦性、模塊性和共享子空間所塑造的低維、高結構的權重空間區域。在這一觀點的基礎上，我們將現有方法組織成五階段管道，調查該方法已經實用的應用，並澄清當前的限制：適配器規模和條件生成正在迅速發展，而不受限制的前沿規模檢查點合成仍然是開放的。我們的目標是將社群的默認思維模式從針對每個任務優化模型轉變為從學習到的權重分佈中抽樣模型，加速邁向一個AI系統常規地改進或創造其他AI系統的時代。

##### **SCICONVBENCH: Benchmarking LLMs on Multi-Turn Clarification for Task Formulation in Computational Science**
2605.18630v1 by Nithin Somasekharan, Youssef Hassan, Shiyao Lin, Gihan Panapitiya, Patrick Emami, Anurag Acharya, Sameera Horawalavithana, Shaowu Pan

Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as scientific AI as- sistants, and a growing body of benchmarks evaluates their capabilities across knowledge retrieval, reasoning, code generation, and tool use. These evaluations, however, typically assume the scientific problem is already well-posed, whereas practical scientific assistance often begins with an ill-posed user request that must be refined through dialogue before any computation, analysis, or experiment can be carried out reliably. We introduce SCICONVBENCH, a benchmark for multi- turn clarification in scientific task formulation across four computational science problem domains: fluid mechanics, solid mechanics, materials science, and par- tial differential equations (PDEs). SCICONVBENCH targets two complementary capabilities: eliciting missing information (disambiguation) and detecting and correcting erroneous requests containing internally contradictory information (in- consistency resolution). Our benchmark pairs a structured task ontology with a rubric-based evaluation framework, enabling systematic measurement of LLM per- formance across three dimensions: clarification behavior, conversational grounding, and final-specification fidelity. Current frontier models perform relatively well on inconsistency resolution, but even the best model resolves only 52.7% of the disambiguation cases in fluid mechanics. We further find that frontier LLMs fre- quently make silent assumptions and perform implicit specification repairs that are not grounded in the conversation with users. SCICONVBENCH establishes a foundation for evaluating the upstream conversational reasoning that a reliable computational science assistant requires. The code and data can be found at https://github.com/csml-rpi/SciConvBench.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）越來越多地被用作科學AI助手，並且越來越多的基準評估它們在知識檢索、推理、代碼生成和工具使用方面的能力。 然而，這些評估通常假設科學問題已經被良好地提出，而實際的科學協助往往始於一個不明確的用戶請求，這必須通過對話來精煉，然後才能可靠地進行計算、分析或實驗。 我們介紹了SCICONVBENCH，這是一個針對科學任務表述中多輪澄清的基準，涵蓋四個計算科學問題領域：流體力學、固體力學、材料科學和偏微分方程（PDEs）。 SCICONVBENCH針對兩種互補的能力：引出缺失信息（消歧義）和檢測及修正包含內部矛盾信息的錯誤請求（不一致性解決）。 我們的基準將結構化任務本體與基於評分標準的評估框架相結合，實現了對LLM性能在三個維度上的系統測量：澄清行為、對話基礎和最終規範的忠實度。 當前的前沿模型在不一致性解決方面表現相對良好，但即使是最好的模型在流體力學中也僅解決了52.7%的消歧義案例。 我們進一步發現，前沿LLMs經常做出默默的假設，並進行隱式的規範修正，這些修正並未在與用戶的對話中得到支持。 SCICONVBENCH為評估可靠的計算科學助手所需的上游對話推理建立了一個基礎。 代碼和數據可以在https://github.com/csml-rpi/SciConvBench找到。

##### **Stochastic Penalty-Barrier Methods for Constrained Machine Learning**
2605.18618v2 by Adam Bosák, Andrii Kliachkin, Jana Lepšová, Gilles Bareilles, Jakub Mareček

Constrained machine learning enables fairness-aware training, physics-informed neural networks, and integration of symbolic domain knowledge into statistical models. Despite its practical importance, no general method exists for the non-convex, non-smooth, stochastic setting that arises naturally in deep learning. We propose the Stochastic Penalty-Barrier Method (SPBM), which extends classical penalty and barrier methods to this setting via exponential dual averaging, a stabilized penalty schedule, and the Moreau envelope to handle non-smoothness. Experiments across multiple settings show that SPBM matches or outperforms existing constrained optimization baselines while incurring only linear runtime overhead compared to unconstrained Adam for up to 10,000 constraints.

摘要：受限機器學習使得公平意識的訓練、物理知識驅動的神經網絡，以及將符號領域知識整合到統計模型中成為可能。儘管其實際重要性不言而喻，但在深度學習中自然出現的非凸、非光滑、隨機設定下，尚不存在通用的方法。我們提出了隨機懲罰障礙法（SPBM），該方法通過指數對偶平均、穩定的懲罰計劃和Moreau包絡來擴展經典的懲罰和障礙方法，以處理非光滑性。多個設定下的實驗顯示，SPBM的表現與現有的受限優化基準相當或更優，且與無限制的Adam相比，僅增加了線性的運行時間開銷，支持多達10,000個約束條件。

##### **CATA: Continual Machine Unlearning via Conflict-Averse Task Arithmetic**
2605.18610v1 by Shen Lin, Junhao Dong, Rongjie Chen, Xiaoyu Zhang, Li Xu, Xiaofeng Chen

Vision-language models (VLMs) have shown remarkable ability in aligning visual and textual representations, enabling a wide range of multimodal applications. However, their large-scale training data inevitably raises concerns about privacy, copyright, and undesirable content, creating a strong need for machine unlearning. While existing studies mainly focus on single-shot unlearning, practical VLM deployment often involves sequential removal requests over time, giving rise to continual machine unlearning. In this work, we make the first attempt to study continual unlearning for VLMs and identify three key challenges in this setting: effectiveness in removing target knowledge, fidelity in preserving retained model utility, and persistence in preventing knowledge re-emergence under sequential updates. To address these challenges, we propose CATA, a conflict-averse task arithmetic method that represents each forget request as an unlearning task vector. By maintaining historical task vectors and performing sign-aware conflict-averse aggregation, CATA suppresses conflicting update components that may weaken previous forgetting effects. Extensive experiments under both single-shot and continual settings show that CATA outperforms baselines in terms of forgetting effectiveness, model fidelity, and forgetting persistence.

摘要：視覺-語言模型 (VLMs) 在對齊視覺和文本表示方面展現了卓越的能力，使得各種多模態應用成為可能。<lb/>然而，它們的大規模訓練數據不可避免地引發了對隱私、版權和不當內容的擔憂，從而強烈需要機器的遺忘。<lb/>雖然現有研究主要集中於單次遺忘，但實際的 VLM 部署往往涉及隨時間進行的連續移除請求，這產生了持續的機器遺忘。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們首次嘗試研究 VLM 的持續遺忘，並在這一背景下確定了三個主要挑戰：有效移除目標知識的能力、保持保留模型效用的忠實度，以及在連續更新下防止知識重新出現的持久性。<lb/>為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了 CATA，一種抗衝突的任務算術方法，將每個遺忘請求表示為一個遺忘任務向量。<lb/>通過維護歷史任務向量並進行符號感知的抗衝突聚合，CATA 抑制可能削弱先前遺忘效果的衝突更新組件。<lb/>在單次和持續設置下的廣泛實驗顯示，CATA 在遺忘有效性、模型忠實度和遺忘持久性方面均優於基準。

##### **AMARIS: A Memory-Augmented Rubric Improvement System for Rubric-Based Reinforcement Learning**
2605.18592v1 by Peilin Wu, Xinlu Zhang, Kun Wan, Wentian Zhao, Gang Wu, Xinya Du, Zhiyu Chen

Rubric-based reward shaping is an effective method for fine-tuning LLMs via RL, where structured rubrics decompose standard outcome rewards into multiple dimensions to provide richer reward signals. Recent works make the rubrics adaptive based on local signals such as the rollouts from the current step or pairwise comparisons. However, these methods discard the diagnostics produced during evaluation after immediate use and prevent the long-term accumulation and strategic reuse of evaluation knowledge. This forces the system to re-derive evaluation principles from scratch, limits its ability to detect recurring suboptimal behaviors, and forfeits the curriculum-like progression that a persistent training history would naturally support. To address these limitations, we introduce AMARIS, which grounds rubric modifications in long-term training history. At each training step, AMARIS analyzes individual rollouts, aggregates findings into step-level summaries, retrieves relevant historical context from a persistent evaluation memory through both static (recent steps) and dynamic (semantically matched) retrieval, and updates rubrics based on these accumulated analyses. This procedure runs asynchronously alongside the normal RL loop with minimal overhead. Experiments across both closed and open-ended domains show that AMARIS consistently outperforms the baselines. Ablation studies show that static and dynamic memory retrieval contributes to the performance gain and their combination provides the strongest results with moderate retrieval budgets sufficient to provide most of the gain, and that the entire pipeline adds only ~5\% time overhead through asynchronous execution. These results show that persistent evaluation memory can transform rubric-based reward shaping from a stateless, per-step heuristic into an evidence-driven loop for RL training.

摘要：基於評分標準的獎勵塑造是一種通過強化學習微調大型語言模型的有效方法，其中結構化的評分標準將標準結果獎勵分解為多個維度，以提供更豐富的獎勵信號。最近的研究使得評分標準根據當前步驟的回饋或成對比較等本地信號變得自適應。然而，這些方法在立即使用後會丟棄評估過程中產生的診斷，並阻止評估知識的長期積累和戰略重用。這迫使系統從頭開始重新推導評估原則，限制了其檢測重複次優行為的能力，並放棄了持久訓練歷史自然支持的課程式進展。為了解決這些限制，我們引入了AMARIS，它將評分標準的修改基於長期訓練歷史。在每個訓練步驟中，AMARIS分析個別回饋，將發現匯總成步驟級摘要，通過靜態（最近步驟）和動態（語義匹配）檢索從持久評估記憶中檢索相關的歷史背景，並根據這些累積的分析更新評分標準。這一過程與正常的強化學習循環異步運行，並且開銷最小。在封閉和開放式領域的實驗顯示，AMARIS始終優於基準。消融研究顯示，靜態和動態記憶檢索對性能增益有貢獻，並且它們的組合在適度的檢索預算下提供了最強的結果，足以提供大部分增益，整個流程通過異步執行僅增加約5\%的時間開銷。這些結果顯示，持久的評估記憶可以將基於評分標準的獎勵塑造從無狀態的逐步啟發式轉變為一個基於證據的強化學習訓練循環。

##### **MA$^{2}$P: A Meta-Cognitive Autonomous Intelligent Agents Framework for Complex Persuasion**
2605.18572v1 by Dingyi Zhang, Ziqing Zhuang, Linhai Zhang, Ziyang Gao, Deyu Zhou

Persuasive dialogue generation plays a vital role in decision-making, negotiation, counseling, and behavior change, yet it remains a challenging problem. In complex persuasion where the persuadee's internal states are not expressed clearly, the persuader must interpret responses, infer the persuadee's latent mental states (e.g., beliefs and desires), and translate them into targeted, strategy-consistent actions; however, current approaches often produce generic or weakly grounded responses even when such cues are identified. Moreover, although large language models (LLMs) can generate persuasive content, their performance varies substantially across domains due to uneven knowledge coverage and limited reasoning generalization. To address these challenges, we propose MA$^{2}$P, a meta-cognitive autonomous intelligent agent framework for complex persuasion. Specifically, we develop an autonomous multi-agent architecture that coordinates perception management, mental-state inference, strategy execution, memory maintenance, and performance evaluation. To mitigate cross-domain performance variation, we further design a meta-cognitive configurator that selects an appropriate meta-strategy from a structured knowledge base at the outset, thereby guiding subsequent reasoning and planning. Experimental results show that our approach achieves a higher persuasion success rate than baselines.

摘要：說服對話生成在決策、談判、輔導和行為變化中扮演著至關重要的角色，但這仍然是一個具有挑戰性的問題。在複雜的說服過程中，當被說服者的內部狀態未明確表達時，說服者必須解釋回應，推斷被說服者的潛在心理狀態（例如，信念和願望），並將其轉化為有針對性且符合策略的行動；然而，當這些線索被識別時，目前的方法往往產生通用或基礎薄弱的回應。此外，儘管大型語言模型（LLMs）可以生成說服性內容，但由於知識覆蓋不均和推理泛化有限，它們在不同領域的表現差異顯著。為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了MA$^{2}$P，一個用於複雜說服的元認知自主智能代理框架。具體而言，我們開發了一個自主多代理架構，協調感知管理、心理狀態推斷、策略執行、記憶維護和性能評估。為了減輕跨領域性能變異，我們進一步設計了一個元認知配置器，該配置器在開始時從結構化知識庫中選擇適當的元策略，從而指導後續的推理和規劃。實驗結果顯示，我們的方法實現了比基準更高的說服成功率。

##### **Query-Conditioned Knowledge Alignment for Reliable Cross-System Medical Reasoning**
2605.18570v1 by Yan Jiao, Jingran Xu, Pin-Han Ho, Limei Peng

Cross-domain knowledge alignment is essential for integrating heterogeneous medical systems, yet existing approaches typically treat entity alignment as a static matching problem, ignoring query context and cross-system asymmetry. This limitation is particularly critical in integrative medical settings, where correspondence between concepts is inherently context-dependent, non-bijective, and direction-sensitive.
  In this paper, we propose Query-Conditioned Entity Alignment (QCEA), which reformulates entity alignment as a query-conditioned correspondence problem. Instead of learning a fixed mapping between entity representations, QCEA treats the textual description of a source entity as a query and ranks candidate entities in the target graph, enabling context-dependent alignment. The framework integrates semantic encoding, graph-based representation learning, and a direction-aware transformation module to capture asymmetric and many-to-many correspondence across heterogeneous knowledge systems.
  We evaluate QCEA on TCM--WM knowledge graphs derived from SymMap, covering both symptom alignment and herb--molecule alignment tasks. Experimental results show consistent improvements over representative baselines, particularly on rank-sensitive metrics such as Hit@K and MRR. Furthermore, downstream retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) experiments demonstrate that improved alignment leads to better evidence retrieval, stronger grounding, and higher answer accuracy. These findings highlight that alignment is not merely a data integration step, but a key factor that shapes knowledge accessibility and reliability in cross-system medical reasoning.

摘要：跨域知識對齊對於整合異質醫療系統至關重要，但現有方法通常將實體對齊視為靜態匹配問題，忽略了查詢上下文和跨系統的不對稱性。這一限制在整合醫療環境中特別關鍵，因為概念之間的對應本質上依賴於上下文、非雙射且對方向敏感。<lb/>在本文中，我們提出了查詢條件實體對齊（QCEA），將實體對齊重新表述為查詢條件的對應問題。QCEA不再學習實體表示之間的固定映射，而是將源實體的文本描述視為查詢，並在目標圖中對候選實體進行排名，實現上下文依賴的對齊。該框架整合了語義編碼、基於圖的表示學習和一個方向感知的轉換模塊，以捕捉異質知識系統之間的不對稱和多對多的對應關係。<lb/>我們在從SymMap衍生的中醫-西醫知識圖上評估QCEA，涵蓋症狀對齊和草藥-分子對齊任務。實驗結果顯示在代表性基準上有一致的改進，特別是在對排名敏感的指標如Hit@K和MRR上。此外，下游檢索增強生成（RAG）實驗表明，改進的對齊導致更好的證據檢索、更強的基礎支持和更高的答案準確性。這些發現強調了對齊不僅僅是一個數據整合步驟，而是影響跨系統醫療推理中知識可及性和可靠性的關鍵因素。

##### **GUT-IS: A Data-Driven Approach to Integrating Constructs and Their Relations in Information Systems**
2605.18567v1 by Maximilian Reinhardt, Jonas Scharfenberger, Burkhardt Funk

Structural equation modeling is widely used in IS research. However, inconsistent construct definitions impede the cumulative development of knowledge. In this work, we present an approach that aims at the integration of structural equation models into a unified model: We use a combination of task-adapted text embeddings and clustering to produce a candidate set of construct groupings. Subsequently, we select the optimal solution using a loss function that explicitly trades off semantic purity and parsimony in the number of clusters. By making this trade-off explicit, our approach allows to analyze how construct groupings and their relations change as one shifts the priority from purity to parsimony. Empirically, we evaluate and explore the proposed methodology on two datasets from the IS domain.

摘要：結構方程式模型在資訊系統研究中被廣泛使用。然而，不一致的構念定義妨礙了知識的累積發展。在這項工作中，我們提出一種旨在將結構方程式模型整合到統一模型中的方法：我們使用任務適應的文本嵌入和聚類的組合來生成構念分組的候選集。隨後，我們使用一個損失函數來選擇最佳解，該函數明確地在語義純度和聚類數量的簡約性之間進行權衡。通過使這一權衡明確，我們的方法允許分析構念分組及其關係如何隨著優先考慮從純度轉向簡約性而變化。實證上，我們在來自資訊系統領域的兩個數據集上評估和探索所提出的方法。

##### **Key-Gram: Extensible World Knowledge for Embodied Manipulation**
2605.18556v1 by Jingjing Fan, Siyuan Li, Botao Ren, Zhidong Deng

Embodied control increasingly requires models to follow compositional language instructions while reasoning over dynamic visual states. However, current vision-language-action policies and world-action models often couple linguistic knowledge with visual computation in a shared backbone or conditioning pathway, leading to modality competition and making knowledge extension dependent on backbone updates. In this paper, we introduce Key-Gram, a conditional-memory framework that separates language-derived world knowledge from visual-state reasoning for embodied control. At its core is a memory module that decomposes an instruction into task-specific key-grams, retrieves static linguistic priors through deterministic hashed lookup, and injects the retrieved entries into selected hidden layers through context-aware gating and lightweight convolutional fusion. This design allows the backbone to devote its main capacity to visual reasoning and action inference, while reusable instruction knowledge is stored in an extensible external memory. The logical memory table can be conveniently partitioned during training and, due to its $O(1)$ lookup pattern, efficiently placed on host memory during inference. Across RoboTwin2.0, LIBERO/LIBERO-Plus, and real-world dual-arm manipulation, Key-Gram consistently improves both $π_{0}$ and $π_{0.5}$ backbones, with average relative gains of $29.5\%/9.9\%$ on RoboTwin2.0, $35.8\%/4.5\%$ on LIBERO-Plus transfer without target-domain fine-tuning, and $15.4\%/8.1\%$ on real-world long-horizon tasks. These results demonstrate that externalized linguistic memory provides an effective and extensible mechanism for improving compositional grounding, transfer, and real-world manipulation.

摘要：具身控制越來越需要模型在推理動態視覺狀態的同時，遵循組合語言指令。<lb/>然而，當前的視覺-語言-行動政策和世界-行動模型通常將語言知識與視覺計算結合在一個共享的骨幹或條件路徑中，導致模態競爭，並使知識擴展依賴於骨幹更新。<lb/>在本文中，我們介紹了Key-Gram，一個條件記憶框架，將語言衍生的世界知識與視覺狀態推理分離，以實現具身控制。<lb/>其核心是一個記憶模塊，將指令分解為任務特定的關鍵語素，通過確定性哈希查找檢索靜態語言先驗，並通過上下文感知的閘控和輕量級卷積融合將檢索到的條目注入選定的隱藏層。<lb/>這種設計使得骨幹可以將其主要能力專注於視覺推理和行動推斷，而可重用的指令知識則存儲在可擴展的外部記憶中。<lb/>邏輯記憶表在訓練過程中可以方便地進行分區，並且由於其$O(1)$查找模式，在推理過程中可以高效地放置在主機記憶中。<lb/>在RoboTwin2.0、LIBERO/LIBERO-Plus和現實世界的雙臂操作中，Key-Gram始終改善了$π_{0}$和$π_{0.5}$骨幹，RoboTwin2.0的平均相對增益為$29.5\%/9.9\%$，LIBERO-Plus轉移的平均相對增益為$35.8\%/4.5\%$，而在現實世界的長期任務中為$15.4\%/8.1\%$。<lb/>這些結果表明，外部化的語言記憶提供了一種有效且可擴展的機制，用於改善組合基礎、轉移和現實世界的操作。

##### **EvoMemBench: Benchmarking Agent Memory from a Self-Evolving Perspective**
2605.18421v1 by Yuyao Wang, Zhongjian Zhang, Mo Chi, Kaichi Yu, Yuhan Li, Miao Peng, Bing Tong, Chen Zhang, Yan Zhou, Jia Li

Recent benchmarks for Large Language Model (LLM) agents mainly evaluate reasoning, planning, and execution. However, memory is also essential for agents, as it enables them to store, update, and retrieve information over time. This ability remains under-evaluated, largely because existing benchmarks do not provide a systematic way to assess memory mechanisms. In this paper, we study agent memory from a self-evolving perspective and introduce EvoMemBench, a unified benchmark organized along two axes: memory scope (in-episode vs. cross-episode) and memory content (knowledge-oriented vs. execution-oriented). We compare 15 representative memory methods with strong long-context baselines under a standardized protocol. Results show that current memory systems are still far from a general solution: long-context baselines remain highly competitive, memory helps most when the current context is insufficient or tasks are difficult, and no single memory form works consistently across all settings. Retrieval-based methods remain strong for knowledge-intensive settings, whereas procedural and long-term memory methods are more effective for execution-oriented tasks when their stored experience matches the task structure. We hope EvoMemBench facilitates future research on more effective memory systems for LLM-based agents. Our code is available at https://github.com/DSAIL-Memory/EvoMemBench.

摘要：最近針對大型語言模型（LLM）代理的基準主要評估推理、規劃和執行。然而，記憶對於代理來說也是至關重要的，因為它使代理能夠隨著時間的推移存儲、更新和檢索信息。這種能力仍然被低估，主要是因為現有的基準未能提供系統性的方法來評估記憶機制。在本文中，我們從自我演化的角度研究代理記憶，並介紹EvoMemBench，一個沿著兩個軸組織的統一基準：記憶範圍（在劇集內 vs. 跨劇集）和記憶內容（知識導向 vs. 執行導向）。我們在標準化協議下比較了15種具有代表性的記憶方法，並與強大的長上下文基線進行對比。結果顯示，當前的記憶系統仍然遠未達到通用解決方案：長上下文基線仍然具有高度競爭力，記憶在當前上下文不足或任務困難時幫助最大，而沒有任何單一的記憶形式在所有設置中都能穩定運作。基於檢索的方法在知識密集型的設置中仍然強勁，而程序性和長期記憶方法在其存儲的經驗與任務結構匹配時對於執行導向任務更為有效。我們希望EvoMemBench能促進未來對於基於LLM的代理更有效的記憶系統的研究。我們的代碼可在 https://github.com/DSAIL-Memory/EvoMemBench 獲得。

##### **Graph Hierarchical Recurrence for Long-Range Generalization**
2605.18387v1 by Stefano Carotti, Marco Pacini, Alessio Gravina, Davide Bacciu, Bruno Lepri, Sebastiano Bontorin

Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) and Graph Transformers (GTs) are now a fundamental paradigm for graph learning, combining the representation-learning capabilities of deep models with the sample efficiency induced by their inductive biases. Despite their effectiveness, a large body of work has shown that these models still face fundamental limitations in tasks that require capturing correlations between distant regions of a graph. To address this issue, we introduce Graph Hierarchical Recurrence (GHR), a novel framework that operates jointly on the input graph and on a hierarchical abstraction obtained through pooling. We also show that the limitations of existing models are even more pronounced in out-of-range generalization, where test instances involve interactions over distances longer than those observed during training. By contrast, despite its simple design, GHR provides three key advantages: strong performance on long-range dependencies, improved out-of-range generalization, and high parameter efficiency. To corroborate these claims, we show that across a broad set of long-range benchmarks, GHR consistently outperforms existing graph models while using as little as 1% of the parameters of current state-of-the-art models. These results suggest a complementary direction to the current trend of scaling architectures to obtain graph foundation models, indicating that increased model capacity alone may not be sufficient for generalization.

摘要：圖神經網絡（GNNs）和圖轉換器（GTs）現在已成為圖學習的基本範式，結合了深度模型的表示學習能力和其歸納偏見所帶來的樣本效率。儘管它們的有效性，許多研究表明這些模型在需要捕捉圖中遠端區域之間的相關性的任務中仍然面臨根本性限制。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了圖層次重複（GHR），這是一個新穎的框架，能夠同時在輸入圖和通過池化獲得的層次抽象上運作。我們還顯示，現有模型的限制在超範圍泛化中更加明顯，在這種情況下，測試實例涉及的交互距離超過了訓練期間觀察到的距離。相比之下，儘管其設計簡單，GHR提供了三個關鍵優勢：在長距離依賴性上的強大性能、改善的超範圍泛化和高參數效率。為了證實這些主張，我們展示了在一組廣泛的長距離基準測試中，GHR始終優於現有的圖模型，同時僅使用當前最先進模型的1%的參數。這些結果表明了一種與當前擴展架構以獲得圖基礎模型的趨勢互補的方向，顯示僅僅增加模型容量可能不足以實現泛化。

##### **Instance Discrimination for Link Prediction**
2605.20257v1 by Valentin Cuzin-Rambaud, Mathieu Lefort, Rémy Cazabet

Recently, instance discrimination models have emerged as a major solution for self-supervised learning. Having already demonstrated its effectiveness in the image domain, instance discrimination learning is now proving equally convincing in the graph domain, in particular for node classification. However, fewer contributions have tackled the link prediction task. In this contribution, we propose to adapt existing methods to this context. We first provide a rigorous evaluation of existing self-supervised models in the field of link prediction, showing that the main performance depends on the augmentation process (like in computer vision). We then propose a new structural augmentation based on the community structure that is relevant for link prediction. Our main contribution introduces two new models, L-GRACE and L-BGRL, based on link representations instead of node representations, which improve the performance of the existing methods, especially on unattributed graphs, and we show that they perform on par with the state of the art, both in supervised and self-supervised contexts.

##### **The Hidden Cost of Contextual Sycophancy: an AI Literacy Intervention in Human-AI Collaboration**
2605.18372v1 by Cansu Koyuturk, Sabrina Guidotti, Dimitri Ognibene

Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used in educational settings as interactive tools for collaboration. However, their tendency toward sycophancy, aligning with user beliefs even when incorrect, raises concerns for learning and decision-making, especially for less knowledgeable users. This study investigates how sycophantic alignment emerges in authentic multi-turn human-AI interactions and whether interventions targeting increasing AI literacy and prompting competencies can mitigate its effects. In a controlled mixed-design experiment, 60 participants completed analytical survival ranking tasks by first generating individual rankings and then making final decisions after collaborating with an AI assistant, both before and after receiving either general or sycophancy-focused prompting training. Preliminary results show that LLMs are highly sensitive to user input: lower-quality initial responses lead to poorer AI advice, suggesting that the model mirrors or incorporates user reasoning rather than correcting it or offering better alternatives that are missing or less frequent in the conversation. Critically, the propagation of user errors into AI responses significantly reduced both the quality of AI feedback and final user task performance, revealing a form of contextual sycophantic dependence. While the intervention did not eliminate the propagation of contextual errors, it significantly improved AI advice by reducing the direct mirroring of incorrect user rankings. These findings suggest that prompting and AI literacy alone may be insufficient to ensure epistemically independent AI support, highlighting the need for system-level approaches that better promote critical engagement in human-AI collaboration.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在教育環境中越來越多地被用作互動工具以促進合作。<lb/>然而，它們對於迎合用戶信念的傾向，即使在錯誤的情況下，也引發了對學習和決策的擔憂，特別是對於知識較少的用戶。<lb/>本研究探討了在真實的多輪人機互動中，迎合性對齊是如何產生的，以及針對提高AI素養和提示能力的干預措施是否能減輕其影響。<lb/>在一項控制的混合設計實驗中，60名參與者完成了分析生存排名任務，首先生成個人排名，然後在與AI助手合作後做出最終決策，這一過程在接受一般提示或專注於迎合的提示訓練之前和之後均有進行。<lb/>初步結果顯示，LLMs對用戶輸入非常敏感：質量較低的初始反應導致較差的AI建議，這表明模型反映或納入用戶推理，而不是糾正它或提供在對話中缺失或較少的更好替代方案。<lb/>關鍵是，用戶錯誤在AI反應中的傳播顯著降低了AI反饋的質量和最終用戶任務表現，顯示出一種情境迎合依賴的形式。<lb/>雖然干預措施並未消除情境錯誤的傳播，但它通過減少對不正確用戶排名的直接反映，顯著改善了AI建議。<lb/>這些發現表明，僅僅依賴提示和AI素養可能不足以確保認識上獨立的AI支持，突顯了需要系統層面的方法來更好地促進人機合作中的批判性參與。

##### **CommitDistill: A Lightweight Knowledge-Centric Memory Layer for Software Repositories**
2605.18284v1 by Divya Chukkapalli, Thejesh Avula, Aditya Aggarwal, Harsimran Singh, Amith Tallanki

Software repositories accumulate large amounts of unstructured knowledge in commit messages, pull-request discussions, and issue threads, but developers and AI coding assistants rarely reuse this history effectively. Recent work on typed-memory architectures for LLM agents (MemGPT, generative agents, and the PlugMem module of Yang et al.) argues that agent memory should be distilled, typed knowledge rather than raw interaction text. We adapt that stance to a software repository's own git history under a constrained regime: deterministic, dependency-free, local-only, no embeddings. We present CommitDistill, an open-source Python prototype that mines a local git history into typed knowledge units (Facts, Skills, Patterns) using deterministic regex and surfaces them through a TF-IDF retriever with a calibrated silence threshold (theta = 2.5) that abstains on out-of-distribution queries. The artefact is a trust-instrumented memory substrate: deterministic, no external service, inspectable plain-JSON store, tunable abstention. A case study on five public repositories spanning Python, JavaScript, C, and Java (25,000 commits, 1,167 extracted units) reports useful-precision 0.525 at Cohen's kappa = 0.633 on 40 dual-annotated Python units. The decisive finding is budget-constrained retrieval: at a 256-character per-query budget, CommitDistill reaches 0.750 hit-rate on a 12-query benchmark against BM25's 0.333 and git log --grep's 0.083. On a four-arm paired LLM-as-judge evaluation (n=200 time-travel bug-fixes, two judges) covering control, CommitDistill, a body-budget-matched CD-Hybrid, and BM25, no condition produces a statistically detectable lift over control on the headline mean and CD-Hybrid is indistinguishable from BM25 head-to-head. Extraction over 10,000 commits completes in under 4 seconds on a laptop. Source, annotations, baselines, and a reproducibility script accompany this paper.

摘要：軟體倉庫在提交訊息、拉取請求討論和問題線程中積累了大量非結構化知識，但開發者和 AI 編碼助手很少有效地重用這些歷史。最近針對 LLM 代理的類型記憶架構（MemGPT、生成代理以及 Yang 等人的 PlugMem 模組）的研究認為，代理記憶應該是提煉過的類型知識，而不是原始的互動文本。我們將這一立場調整為軟體倉庫自身的 git 歷史，並在一個受限的體系下進行：確定性、無依賴、僅限本地、無嵌入。我們提出了 CommitDistill，一個開源的 Python 原型，將本地 git 歷史挖掘為類型知識單元（事實、技能、模式），使用確定性正則表達式並通過具有校準靜默閾值（theta = 2.5）的 TF-IDF 檢索器顯示這些單元，對於超出分佈的查詢則不進行回應。這一產物是一個受信任的記憶基質：確定性、無外部服務、可檢查的純 JSON 存儲、可調整的棄權。在涵蓋 Python、JavaScript、C 和 Java 的五個公共倉庫（25,000 次提交，1,167 個提取單元）的案例研究中，對 40 個雙重標註的 Python 單元報告有用精度為 0.525，Cohen's kappa 為 0.633。決定性的發現是預算受限的檢索：在每個查詢 256 字符的預算下，CommitDistill 在 12 次查詢基準上達到 0.750 的命中率，而 BM25 為 0.333，git log --grep 為 0.083。在一個四臂配對的 LLM 作為評判的評估中（n=200 次時間旅行的錯誤修正，兩位評判），涵蓋了控制組、CommitDistill、一個與身體預算匹配的 CD-Hybrid 和 BM25，沒有條件在標題均值上產生統計上可檢測的提升，且 CD-Hybrid 與 BM25 面對面無法區分。在一台筆記本電腦上，對 10,000 次提交的提取在 4 秒內完成。本文附有來源、註釋、基線和可重現性腳本。

##### **Knowledge-to-Verification: Exploring RLVR for LLMs in Knowledge-Intensive Domains**
2605.18261v1 by Zhonghang Yuan, Zhefan Wang, Fang Hu, Zihong Chen, Jinzhe Li, Gang Li, Jie Ying, Huanjun Kong, Songyang Zhang, Nanqing Dong

Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has demonstrated promising potential to enhance the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs) in domains such as mathematics and coding. However, its applications on knowledge-intensive domains have not been effectively explored due to the scarcity of high-quality verifiable data. Furthermore, current RLVR focuses solely on the correctness of final answers, leading to the limitations of flawed reasoning and sparse reward signals. In this work, we propose Knowledge-to-Verification (K2V), a framework that extends RLVR to knowledge-intensive domains through automated verifiable data synthesis, while enabling verification of the LLM's reasoning process. Extensive experiments demonstrate that K2V enhances the reasoning of LLM in knowledge-intensive domains without significantly compromising the model's general capabilities. This study also suggests that integrating automated data synthesis with reasoning verification is a promising direction to enhance model capabilities in these broader domains. Code is available at https://github.com/SeedScientist/K2V.

摘要：強化學習與可驗證獎勵（RLVR）已顯示出在數學和編碼等領域增強大型語言模型（LLMs）推理能力的良好潛力。<lb/>然而，由於高質量可驗證數據的稀缺，其在知識密集型領域的應用尚未得到有效探索。<lb/>此外，目前的RLVR僅專注於最終答案的正確性，這導致了推理缺陷和稀疏獎勵信號的限制。<lb/>在本研究中，我們提出了知識到驗證（K2V）框架，通過自動化可驗證數據合成將RLVR擴展到知識密集型領域，同時實現對LLM推理過程的驗證。<lb/>大量實驗表明，K2V在知識密集型領域增強了LLM的推理能力，而不會顯著損害模型的一般能力。<lb/>本研究還表明，將自動化數據合成與推理驗證相結合是一個有前景的方向，可以增強模型在這些更廣泛領域的能力。<lb/>代碼可在 https://github.com/SeedScientist/K2V 獲得。

##### **Machine Unlearning for Masked Diffusion Language Models**
2605.18253v1 by Georu Lee, Seungwon Jeong, Hoki Kim, Jinseong Park, Woojin Lee

Recent masked diffusion language models (MDLMs), such as LLaDA and Dream, have achieved performance comparable to autoregressive large language models. Unlike autoregressive models, which generate text sequentially, MDLMs generate text by iteratively denoising masked positions in parallel. During fine-tuning, MDLMs learn to recover responses from masked response states conditioned on a prompt, thereby shifting their predictions from a prompt-masked unconditional distribution toward a prompt-conditional distribution. Despite this distinct generative and fine-tuning mechanism, machine unlearning for MDLMs remains largely unexplored. In this paper, we propose Masked Diffusion Unlearning (MDU), the first unlearning framework for MDLMs, by revisiting the process of learning specific knowledge in terms of diffusion. Specifically, MDU minimizes a forward KL divergence from the prompt-conditional prediction to a prompt-masked unconditional anchor at every masked response position, with a temperature scaling parameter to control the privacy-utility trade-off. Our empirical results on standard benchmarks and MDLM backbones show that MDU achieves high unlearning performance compared to existing LLM unlearning methods. Code is available at https://github.com/leegeoru/MDU.

摘要：最近的遮罩擴散語言模型（MDLMs），如LLaDA和Dream，已達到與自回歸大型語言模型相當的性能。與自回歸模型逐步生成文本不同，MDLMs通過迭代去噪平行的遮罩位置來生成文本。在微調過程中，MDLMs學會根據提示從被遮罩的回應狀態中恢復回應，從而將其預測從提示遮罩的無條件分佈轉變為提示條件的分佈。儘管這種生成和微調機制截然不同，但對於MDLMs的機器去學習仍然基本上未被探索。在本文中，我們提出了遮罩擴散去學習（MDU），這是MDLMs的第一個去學習框架，通過重新考慮擴散過程中學習特定知識的過程。具體而言，MDU在每個被遮罩的回應位置最小化從提示條件預測到提示遮罩的無條件錨點的前向KL散度，並使用溫度縮放參數來控制隱私與效用的權衡。我們在標準基準和MDLM骨幹上的實證結果顯示，與現有的LLM去學習方法相比，MDU實現了高效的去學習性能。代碼可在https://github.com/leegeoru/MDU獲得。

##### **Leveraging Graph Structure in Seq2Seq Models for Knowledge Graph Link Prediction**
2605.18211v1 by Luu Huu Phuc, Ratan Bahadur Thapa, Mojtaba Nayyeri, Jingcheng Wu, Evgeny Kharlamov, Steffen Staab

We introduce Graph-Augmented Sequence-to-Sequence (GA-S2S), a novel framework that integrates a T5-small encoder-decoder with a Relational Graph Attention Network (RGAT) to improve link prediction in knowledge graphs. While existing Seq2Seq models rely solely on surface-level textual descriptions of entities and relations and at best, flatten the neighborhoods of a query entity into a single linear sequence, thereby discarding the inherent graph structure, GA-S2S jointly encodes both textual features and the full $k$-hop subgraph topology surrounding the query entity. By integrating raw encoder outputs with RGAT's relation-aware embeddings, our model captures and leverages richer multi-hop relational patterns and textual information. Our preliminary experiments on the CoDEx dataset demonstrate that GA-S2S outperforms competitive Seq2Seq-based baseline models, achieving up to a 19\% relative gain in link prediction accuracy.

摘要：我們介紹了圖增強序列到序列（GA-S2S），這是一個新穎的框架，將T5-small編碼器-解碼器與關係圖注意力網絡（RGAT）結合，以改善知識圖譜中的連結預測。雖然現有的Seq2Seq模型僅依賴於實體和關係的表面文本描述，並且在最佳情況下將查詢實體的鄰域壓縮為單一線性序列，從而丟棄了固有的圖結構，但GA-S2S則共同編碼文本特徵和圍繞查詢實體的完整$k$-跳子圖拓撲。通過將原始編碼器輸出與RGAT的關係感知嵌入相結合，我們的模型捕捉並利用了更豐富的多跳關係模式和文本信息。我們在CoDEx數據集上的初步實驗表明，GA-S2S超越了競爭性的基於Seq2Seq的基準模型，在連結預測準確性上實現了高達19\%的相對增益。

##### **Concise and Logically Consistent Conformal Sets for Neuro-Symbolic Concept-Based Models**
2605.18202v1 by Samuele Bortolotti, Emanuele Marconato, Andrea Pugnana, Andrea Passerini, Stefano Teso

Neuro-Symbolic Concept-based Models (NeSy-CBMs) are a family of architectures that integrate neural networks with symbolic reasoning for enhanced reliability in high-stakes applications. They work by first extracting high-level concepts from the input and then inferring a task label from these compatibly with given logical constraints. Yet, their label and concept predictions can be overconfident, making it difficult for stakeholders to gauge when the model's decisions can be trusted. We address this issue by integrating ideas from Conformal Prediction (CP), a framework providing rigorous, distribution-free coverage guarantees. We formalize three desiderata -- consistency, coverage, and conciseness -- that any conformal method for NeSy-CBMs should satisfy, and show that existing approaches fall short of at least one. We then introduce COCOCO, a post-hoc framework that conformalizes concepts and labels jointly and reconciles them via a single deduction-abduction revision step. COCOCO satisfies all three desiderata, retains distribution-free coverage, is robust to imperfect knowledge and supports user-specified size budgets. Our experiments on 8 data sets highlight how COCOCO compares favorably against competitors and natural baselines in terms of performance and set size.

摘要：神經符號概念模型（NeSy-CBMs）是一類將神經網絡與符號推理相結合的架構，以增強在高風險應用中的可靠性。它們的工作方式是首先從輸入中提取高層次的概念，然後根據給定的邏輯約束推斷任務標籤。然而，它們的標籤和概念預測可能過於自信，使利益相關者難以評估模型的決策何時可以信任。我們通過整合符合預測（CP）的思想來解決這個問題，這是一個提供嚴格的無分佈覆蓋保證的框架。我們形式化了三個期望——一致性、覆蓋性和簡潔性——任何適合NeSy-CBMs的符合方法應該滿足這些期望，並顯示現有方法至少在一個方面不足。我們然後介紹了COCOCO，一個後處理框架，該框架共同符合概念和標籤，並通過單一的推導-反推修正步驟進行調和。COCOCO滿足所有三個期望，保持無分佈覆蓋，對不完美知識具有穩健性，並支持用戶指定的大小預算。我們在8個數據集上的實驗突顯了COCOCO在性能和集合大小方面相較於競爭對手和自然基準的優勢。

##### **Fixed External Cameras as Common Prior Maps for Active 3D Scene Graph Generation**
2605.18184v1 by Giorgia Modi, Davide Buoso, Giuseppe Averta, Daniele De Martini

Commonly available prior information, such as BIM models, floor plans, and remote sensing images, can provide valuable geometric and semantic context for autonomous robotic systems. In this paper, we treat observations from fixed external RGB cameras as Common Prior Maps (CPMs): wide-field views of the environment that initialize a semantic and geometric scene prior before any robot motion begins. We present an RGB-only framework for active, incremental 3D scene graph (3DSG) generation that seamlessly fuses observations from both onboard robot cameras and fixed external cameras within a single hardware-agnostic pipeline. By relying solely on RGB observations processed by a feed-forward 3D reconstruction model, the system treats all cameras - onboard or external - identically, requiring no hardware modifications. A graph-based active semantic exploration framework then directly leverages the partial scene graph to guide the robot toward regions of high semantic uncertainty, progressively completing and refining the prior. Experiments demonstrate that bootstrapping the scene graph with even a single external camera increases initial object recall by up to +79%, and that the richer context of the prior significantly improves the efficiency of subsequent active exploration.

摘要：常見的可用先前資訊，例如BIM模型、平面圖和遙感影像，可以為自主機器人系統提供有價值的幾何和語義背景。<lb/>在本文中，我們將來自固定外部RGB相機的觀測視為共通先前地圖（CPMs）：環境的廣角視圖，在任何機器人運動開始之前初始化語義和幾何場景的先驗。<lb/>我們提出了一個僅基於RGB的框架，用於主動的增量3D場景圖（3DSG）生成，該框架在單一的硬體無關管道中無縫融合來自機器人機載相機和固定外部相機的觀測。<lb/>通過僅依賴由前饋3D重建模型處理的RGB觀測，系統將所有相機（無論是機載還是外部）視為相同，無需硬體修改。<lb/>基於圖形的主動語義探索框架隨後直接利用部分場景圖，引導機器人朝向高語義不確定性的區域，逐步完成和精煉先驗。<lb/>實驗表明，即使用一個外部相機啟動場景圖，也能將初始物體召回率提高多達79%，而且先驗的豐富背景顯著提高了隨後主動探索的效率。

##### **Evidence-Grounded Frontier Mapping and Agentic Hypothesis Generation in Nanomedicine**
2605.18144v1 by Christiaan G. A. Viviers, Koen de Bruin, Mirre M. Trines, Ayla M. Hokke, Roy van der Meel, Avi Schroeder, Twan Lammers, Willem J. M. Mulder, Fons van der Sommen

Nanomedicine research spans delivery chemistry, immunology, imaging, biomaterials, and disease-specific translational science, yet its conceptual design space remains fragmented across a large and heterogeneous literature. To date, artificial intelligence in nanomedicine has focused primarily on property prediction and formulation optimization, with much less attention to evidence-grounded discovery support at the level of research direction selection. We introduce pArticleMap, a literature-mapping and research-hypothesis-generation system that combines article embeddings, similarity-graph analysis, sparse frontier extraction, structured evidence-pack retrieval, and an audited large-language-model (LLM) workflow for grounded ideation. Rather than forecasting future concept co-occurrence, pArticleMap targets low-density article-level bridge regions and cluster interfaces, then generates and scores citation-grounded hypotheses with large language models in an agentic setup. We evaluate the system with a retrospective realization benchmark (generate later literature under a historical cutoff) and a blinded human reader assessment layer across cue-conditioned nanomedicine tasks. Across 4 selected retrospective bundles, pArticleMap generated ideas and selected task-retained hypotheses (winner ideas) under the benchmark protocol. For task-level retained hypotheses, a pooled gold recovery rate of 10.8% was obtained, with a recall@10 of 15.9% and a future-neighborhood rate of 61.0%, indicating that the system often reached the correct forward-looking neighborhood (paper ideas) even without exact paper-level recovery. Human-agent agreement is modest overall, indicating that internal scoring is useful as a support signal but does not replace expert judgment. These results position pArticleMap as a conservative, evidence-grounded research assistant for nanomedicine.

摘要：奈米醫學研究涵蓋了傳遞化學、免疫學、影像學、生物材料以及特定疾病的轉譯科學，但其概念設計空間在大量異質文獻中仍然分散。迄今為止，奈米醫學中的人工智慧主要集中在性質預測和配方優化上，而對於基於證據的發現支持在研究方向選擇層面上則關注較少。我們介紹了 pArticleMap，這是一個文獻映射和研究假設生成系統，結合了文章嵌入、相似性圖分析、稀疏邊界提取、結構化證據包檢索以及經過審核的大型語言模型（LLM）工作流程以支持有根據的創意。pArticleMap 的目標不是預測未來概念的共現，而是針對低密度的文章級橋接區域和集群界面，然後在代理設置中生成並評分基於引用的假設。 我們通過回顧性實現基準（在歷史截止日期下生成後續文獻）和一個盲人讀者評估層來評估該系統，涵蓋了以提示為條件的奈米醫學任務。在四個選定的回顧性捆綁中，pArticleMap 在基準協議下生成了想法並選擇了任務保留的假設（獲勝想法）。對於任務級保留的假設，獲得了 10.8% 的總金回收率，召回率@10 為 15.9%，未來鄰域率為 61.0%，這表明該系統即使在沒有精確的文章級回收的情況下，仍然經常達到正確的前瞻性鄰域（論文想法）。人類與代理的協議整體上是適度的，這表明內部評分作為支持信號是有用的，但並不能取代專家的判斷。這些結果使 pArticleMap 成為奈米醫學中一個保守的、基於證據的研究助手。

##### **Generative AI and the Productivity Divide: Human-AI Complementarities in Education**
2605.18143v1 by Lihi Idan, Bharat Anand

Generative Artificial Intelligence (GenAI) is transforming how firms create, process, and apply knowledge, yet little is known about the heterogeneity of its productivity effects across users. We report results from a randomized controlled experiment in which participants-analogs of early-career knowledge workers-were assigned to self-study a technical domain using either traditional resources or large-language-model (LLM) assistance. On average, GenAI access significantly increased task performance, but the distribution of gains was highly uneven. Improvements were not predicted by GPA or prior knowledge, but by \textit{AI Interaction Competence (AIC)} -- the ability to elicit, filter, and verify model outputs. High-AIC participants realized outsized gains; low-AIC participants saw limited or even negative marginal returns. A scaffolding intervention (conceptual maps) reduced outcome variance, indicating that standardized workflows can mitigate inequality in AI-mediated performance. We interpret these findings through the lens of human-AI complementarities: GenAI raises mean productivity while introducing a new axis of capability inequality. Managerially, firms should pair GenAI access with short AIC micro-training and simple standard operating procedures to capture value consistently and avoid uneven adoption outcomes.

摘要：生成性人工智慧（GenAI）正在改變企業創造、處理和應用知識的方式，但對於其在用戶之間生產力效應的異質性知之甚少。我們報告了一項隨機對照實驗的結果，參與者是早期職業知識工作者的類比，他們被分配使用傳統資源或大型語言模型（LLM）輔助自學一個技術領域。平均而言，GenAI的使用顯著提高了任務表現，但收益的分佈非常不均。改善的預測並不是基於GPA或先前知識，而是基於\textit{AI互動能力（AIC）}——即引出、過濾和驗證模型輸出的能力。高AIC的參與者獲得了超額收益；低AIC的參與者則看到有限甚至是負的邊際回報。一項支架干預（概念圖）減少了結果的變異，表明標準化工作流程可以減輕AI介導表現中的不平等。我們通過人類與AI的互補性來解釋這些發現：GenAI提高了平均生產力，同時引入了一個新的能力不平等軸。在管理上，企業應該將GenAI的使用與短期AIC微訓練和簡單的標準作業程序相結合，以穩定地捕捉價值並避免不均等的採用結果。

##### **Who Generated This 3D Asset? Learning Source Attribution for Generative 3D Models**
2605.18132v1 by Sihan Ma, Siyuan Liang, Dacheng Tao

Generative 3D models are deployed in gaming, robotics, and immersive creation, making source attribution critical: given a 3D asset, can we identify whether and which generative model created it? This problem faces two core challenges: dispersed attribution signals, where 3D fingerprints are distributed across multi-view, geometric, and frequency-domain cues; and realistic deployment constraints, where scarce labels, degraded prompts, and mixed real/synthetic assets undermine attribution reliability. To systematically study this problem, we construct, to the best of our knowledge, the first passive source attribution benchmark for modern generated assets, covering 22 representative 3D generators under standard, few-shot, and realistic deployment protocols. Based on this benchmark, we find that generative 3D models leave two types of stable fingerprints: cross-view inconsistency and structural artifacts reflected in geometric statistics and frequency-domain cues. To capture these dispersed signals, we propose a hierarchical multi-view multi-modal Transformer that fuses appearance, geometric, and frequency-domain features within each view and models global relationships across views. Extensive experiments demonstrate strong performance, achieving 97.22% accuracy under full supervision and 77.17% accuracy with only 1% training data, corresponding to fewer than five samples per generator. These results show that modern 3D generators leave stable and attributable fingerprints, establishing a new benchmark and methodological foundation for trustworthy 3D content provenance.

摘要：生成的3D模型被應用於遊戲、機器人技術和沉浸式創作，使得來源歸屬變得至關重要：給定一個3D資產，我們能否識別出是哪些生成模型創造了它？這個問題面臨兩個核心挑戰：分散的歸屬信號，其中3D指紋分佈在多視角、幾何和頻域線索中；以及現實的部署限制，稀缺的標籤、退化的提示和混合的真實/合成資產削弱了歸屬的可靠性。為了系統性地研究這個問題，我們構建了截至目前為止，針對現代生成資產的首個被動來源歸屬基準，涵蓋22個代表性的3D生成器，並在標準、少量樣本和現實部署協議下進行測試。基於這個基準，我們發現生成的3D模型留下了兩種類型的穩定指紋：跨視角不一致性和反映在幾何統計和頻域線索中的結構性工件。為了捕捉這些分散的信號，我們提出了一種層次化的多視角多模態Transformer，該模型在每個視角中融合外觀、幾何和頻域特徵，並建模視角之間的全局關係。大量實驗顯示出強勁的性能，在完全監督下達到97.22%的準確率，而在僅用1%訓練數據的情況下達到77.17%的準確率，這相當於每個生成器少於五個樣本。這些結果顯示現代3D生成器留下了穩定且可歸屬的指紋，為可信的3D內容來源建立了一個新的基準和方法論基礎。
